Ambasaderi w' Umuryango w' Ubumwe bw' u Burayi mu Rwanda , Nic@@ ola Bell@@ omo , aherutse gushima uko u Rwanda rurimo guhangana n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , yizeza ko uyu muryango uzakomeza gufatanya na rwo muri uru rugamba no mu zindi gahunda z' iterambere .
Yakomeje ashimira ingamba u Rwanda rwafashe mu gukumira no guhangana n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , zirimo gahunda ya guma mu rugo , gukaraba intoki , guhana intera n' izindi nyinshi .
Ambasaderi Bell@@ omo yavuze ko bishimira ubufatanye burambye hagati ya EU n' u Rwanda , bushingiye nanone ku bufatanye hagati y' imigabane ya Afurika n' u Burayi .
Yavuze kandi ko muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus barimo gukorana n' u Rwanda mu kurebera hamwe uko inkunga yakw@@ ifashishwa guhangana n' iki cyorezo .

uzatangira muri Nyakanga .

Umubare w' abatunze miliyoni 1 $ w@@ ikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize
Rep@@ oro y' Ikigo cyitwa Bos@@ ton Con@@ sul@@ t@@ ing Group ( B@@ CG ) , ku butunzi bw' abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare w' abatunze miliyoni imwe y' amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho w@@ ikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Rep@@ oro y' Ikigo cyitwa Bos@@ ton Con@@ sul@@ t@@ ing Group ( B@@ CG ) , ku butunzi bw' abatuye Isi , yerekanye ko umubare w' abatunze miliyoni imwe y' amadolari kuzamura wiyongereye , aho w@@ ikubye gatatu mu myaka 20 ishize .
Iyi raporo yasohotse kuri uyu wa Kane , yerekanye ko mu mpera za 2019 , abarenga miliyoni 24 ku Isi yose , buri umwe afite ubutunzi b@@ ubarirwa nibura muri miliyoni imwe y' amadolari cyangwa kur@@ enzaho ugereranyije na miliyoni 8 .
9 bari bayit@@ unze mu 1999 , bivuze ko bik@@ ubye hafi gatatu .
Mu myaka 20 ishize kandi , ubutunzi bw' abantu ku giti cyabo ku Isi yose bw@@ ikubye hafi gatatu buva kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 80 mu 1999 bugera kuri miliyari ibihumbi $ 2@@ 26 , mu mpera za 2019 .
Ut@@ eranyije ubutunzi bw' abatunze miliyoni y' amadolari ku Isi yose , bungana na 50 % , by' ubutunzi bw' Isi yose mu 2019 .
Abenshi mu batunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , ni abo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Mu 2019 , mu Bushinwa , abatunze nibura miliyoni 1 $ , bik@@ ubye inshuro 29 , ugereranyije na 1999 .
Ibiciro ku isoko by@@ iyongereyeho 10 , 1 % muri Mata 2019
Ikigo cy' igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NIS@@ R ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikom@@ at@@ anyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , by@@ iyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ikigo cy' igihugu gishinzwe ibarurishamibare mu Rwanda ( NIS@@ R ) , cyatangaje ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro bikom@@ at@@ anyirijwe hamwe mu mijyi no mu byaro , by@@ iyongereyeho 10 , 1 % , ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ih@@ induka ry' ibiciro mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 , ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 13 , 1 % , ugereranyije n' ukwezi nk' uku kwa 2019 .
Itangazo ryashyizwe ahagaragara na NIS@@ R , kuwa 10 Gicurasi 2020 , rigaragaza ko bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro by@@ iyongeraho 10 , 1 % mu kwezi kwa Mata 2020 ' ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byazamutseho 18 , 7 % n' ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bis@@ embuye n' itabi byazamutseho 21 , 3 % ' .
Ku rundi ruhande ariko , iyo ugereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ibiciro byag@@ abanutseho 1 , 8 % , ukom@@ atanyije mu mijyi no mu byaro .
NIS@@ R iti " Iri g@@ abanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byag@@ abanutseho 3 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bic@@ anwa byag@@ abanutseho 3 , 3 % " " " " .
Uko ibiciro by@@ azamutse mu mijyi no mu byaro
NIS@@ R yatangaje ko ibiciro mu mijyi by@@ iyongereyeho 8 % mu kwezi gushize kwa Mata 2020 ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ih@@ induka ry' ibiciro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 8 , 5 % .
Ik@@ omeza igira iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro by@@ iyongeraho 8 % mu kwezi kwa Mata , ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byazamutseho 15 , 8 % , ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bis@@ embuye n' itabi byazamutseho 17 , 4 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bic@@ anwa byazamutseho 6 , 5 % " " " " .
Iyo ugereranyije Mata 2020 na Mata 2019 , usanga ibiciro by' ibintu bitarimo ibiribwa n' ibikomoka ku ngufu byar@@ azamutseho 4 , 6 % .
W@@ agereranya ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byag@@ abanutseho 0 , 2 % .
Iri g@@ abanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byag@@ abanutseho 2 , 1 % .
NIS@@ R ivuga ko muri Mata 2020 , ibiciro mu byaro by@@ iyongereyeho 11 , 7 % ugereranyije na Mata 2019 .
Ih@@ induka ry' ibiciro mu byaro mu kwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) ryari ku kigereranyo kingana na 16 , 5 % .
NIS@@ R yagize iti " Bimwe mu byatumye ibiciro by@@ iyongeraho 11 , 7 % mu kwezi kwa Mata ni ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byazamutseho 20 % n' ibiciro by' ibinyobwa bis@@ embuye n' itabi byazamutseho 23 , 2 % " " " " .
Ug@@ ereranyije ukwezi kwa kane ( Mata 2020 ) n' ukwezi kwa gatatu ( Werurwe 2020 ) , ibiciro byag@@ abanutseho 3 % .
Iri g@@ abanuka ahanini ryatewe n' ibiciro by' ibiribwa n' ibinyobwa bidas@@ embuye byag@@ abanutseho 3 , 4 % n' ibiciro by' amazu , amazi , amashanyarazi , gazi n' ibindi bic@@ anwa byag@@ abanutseho 8 % .
Banki z@@ avug@@ uruye inguzanyo za miliyari 25@@ 5 Frw mu korohereza abakiliya mu bihe bya Coronavirus
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 79@@ 52 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 25@@ 5 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma y' ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ko amabanki amaze kuvugurura inguzanyo 79@@ 52 zifite agaciro ka miliyari 25@@ 5 Frw , mu korohereza abakiliya bayo kwishyura , nyuma y' ingaruka ingamba zafashwe mu gukumira Coronavirus zagize ku bukungu bwabo .
Ku wa 18 Werurwe nibwo Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda yatangaje ingamba zirimo kwemerera amabanki gusubiramo amasezerano y' inguzanyo yagiranye n' abakiliya , kugira ngo az@@ oroh@@ ereze aba@@ yab@@ ereyemo imyenda mu gihe cyo kwishyura .
Nka Banki ya Kigali kimwe n' izindi z' ubucuruzi z@@ ashyizeho igihe gishobora kugera ku mezi atatu umuntu ashobora guhabwa at@@ ishyura inguzanyo yahawe cyangwa inyungu zayo , igihe bigaragara ko ibikorwa bye byag@@ izweho ingaruka n' ibi bihe bikomeye .
Imyanzuro y' Akanama ka Komite ishinzwe politiki y' ifaranga yateranye kuri uyu wa 29 Mata 2020 , igaragaza ko kugeza ku wa 10 Mata , amabanki yavug@@ uruye inguzanyo 79@@ 52 mu 8@@ 6@@ 67 z' abari basabye koroh@@ erezwa , zifite agaciro ka miliyari 25@@ 5 Frw .
BNR kandi yari yagabanyije igipimo cy' amafaranga y' ubw@@ izigame banki zit@@ ajya munsi kiba 4 % kivuye kuri 5 % kugira ngo nazo z@@ ifashe izindi nzego z' ubucuruzi z@@ azah@@ ung@@ abanywa na COVID - 19 .
Mu zindi mpinduka Banki Nkuru y' Igihugu yakoze , harimo ko yagabanyije inyungu ku nguzanyo ihabwa amabanki iv@@ anwa kuri 5 % ishyirwa kuri 4 .
5 % , hagamijwe kuz@@ ifasha kugira ngo zikom@@ eze gutanga amafaranga mu baturage bayak@@ eneye muri ibi bihe , no mu bukungu bw' igihugu muri rusange .

Ku Isi yose ubukungu bukomeje kuz@@ ahara ari nayo mpamvu za leta zafashe ingamba zitandukanye zo kwivana mu bibazo .
Nka Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ziherutse gutangaza ko muri iki gihembwe hagati ya Mata na Kamena izag@@ uza miliyari $ 2 , 99@@ 9 , kubera ihungabana ry' ibikorwa n' ingengo n' ingengo y' imari .
Banki y' Isi iherutse gukora ikigereranyo yerekana ko ubukungu bwa Afurika buz@@ asubira inyuma mu buryo bukomeye ku nshuro ya mbere mu myaka 25 biturutse kuri Coronavirus .
Imibare ya Banki y' Isi yo kuwa 9 Mata igaragaza ko ubukungu bwo muri Afurika yo munsi y' Ubut@@ ayu bwa Sahara , bwag@@ izweho ingaruka na Coronavirus ndetse ko buz@@ amanuka ku kigero cya - 2 .

4 % bwariho mu 2019 .

Hagiye gutangizwa ikigega cya miliyari 100 Frw cyo mu kuzahura ubukungu
Mu ngamba zigamije kuzahura ubukungu , u Rwanda rwashyize ingufu mu buhinzi , hategurwa ibih@@ embwe by' ihinga biri imbere ku buryo abahinzi bahabwa amaf@@ umbire n' imbuto kugira ngo haz@@ abon@@ eke umusaruro mwiza bityo igihugu gikom@@ eze kwihaza mu biribwa kin@@ as@@ agurira amasoko .
Ikindi ni ukw@@ ihutisha imishinga yari yaratangiye itanga akazi , cyane iy@@ ' ibikorwa remezo , nk' inyubako n' ibindi .
Ati " Hari imishinga y' imihanda , iy@@ ' amazi , iy@@ ' amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .
Hari kandi gukomeza gushyira ingufu muri gahunda zo gufasha abatishoboye yaba mu kubaha imirimo , kubaha inkunga ku badashobora gukora n' inguzanyo iciriritse ishobora kwifashishwa mu gukora imirimo ibyara inyungu .
Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari n' abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka n' iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kiba@@ fasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .
Ati " Ni ikigega cy@@ afasha amabanki gutanga inguzanyo iciriritse yafasha ibyo byiciro byose kugira ngo big@@ aruke mu kazi by@@ ongere bikor@@ e , bib@@ yar@@ e umusaruro uz@@ agire ingaruka mu kuzamuka k' ubukungu muri rusange .
Yakomeje atangaza ko " Icyo kigega cyar@@ an@@ og@@ ejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo biz@@ amara igihe kugira ngo bw@@ ongere buz@@ anz@@ amuk@@ e kuko ntibit@@ erwa n' uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .
Dr Ndagijimana yavuze muri icyo kigega h@@ ashyizwemo ingamba zihariye zifasha amahoteli kuvugurura amasezerano y' inguzanyo afite mu mabanki akaba igihe kirekire n' inyungu zik@@ agabanuka , ndetse ku buryo mu gihe yatangiye gufungura , abona amafaranga aciriritse kugira ngo imirimo yongere ikore .
Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwag@@ izweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo biz@@ agend@@ erwaho kugira ngo aba@@ birimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bih@@ ut@@ ishe imirimo " " " " .
Ibigo bito n' ibic@@ iriritse nabyo biri mu biz@@ ahabwa inguzanyo n' ingwate kuko ingwate zikunze kuba ikibazo kuri bene ibyo byiciro .
Ni ikigega biteganyijwe ko gishobora kujyamo nka Miliyari 100 Frw avuye muri leta , ariko hag@@ akomeza gushakwa n' abandi bashyiramo amafaranga kugira ngo cyag@@ uke .
Ati " Tur@@ ateganya ko mu gihe cy' icyumweru kimwe cyaba gitangiye " " " " .
Mu kugabanya icyuho kiri hagati y' ibyoherezwa mu mahanga n' ibit@@ um@@ iz@@ wayo , u Rwanda rur@@ ateganya gukomeza guteza imbere ibikorerwa mu Rwanda , abanyarwanda bag@@ akang@@ ukira kubig@@ ura kugira ngo bis@@ imbure ibyo hanze .
Leta nt@@ iteganya kugabanya imirimo
Kuva icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cy@@ atangira , ibigo byinshi cyane iby@@ ' abikorera , byafashe ingamba zitandukanye zigamije gutuma bid@@ afunga imiryango kubera igabanuka ry' amafaranga by@@ inj@@ izaga .
I@@ byinshi byah@@ agaritse abakozi , ibindi byumvikana nabo bag@@ abanyirizwa imishahara .
Dr Ndagijimana avuga ko abikorera bagerageje guhangana n' iki cyorezo , ku buryo n' abag@@ abanya imirimo n' imishahara , bagerageje kwita ku nyungu z' abakozi .

COVID - 19 : Amabwiriza yag@@ en@@ aga amafaranga ntarengwa SACCO zemerewe kubik@@ uriza abanyamuryango yak@@ uweho
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugur@@ izanya ( SAC@@ CO@@ s ) yemerewe kubik@@ uriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Banki Nkuru y' u Rwanda , BNR , yakuyeho amabwiriza yari yashyizeho agena amafaranga ntarengwa amakoperative yo kubitsa no kugur@@ izanya ( SAC@@ CO@@ s ) yemerewe kubik@@ uriza abanyamuryango bayo .
Izo ngamba zari zashyizweho ku wa 24 Werurwe 2020 nyuma y' iminsi ibiri ibikorwa byinshi bih@@ agaritswe , abaturage bagasabwa kuguma mu ngo hirindwa ikwirakwira ry' icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Izo ngamba z@@ avugaga ko nta SACCO yemerewe kurenza amafaranga ibihumbi 150 , abik@@ uzwa n' umunyamuryango umwe usanzwe , mu cyumweru .
SACCO kandi ntabwo yari yemerewe kubik@@ uriza arenze ibihumbi 500 Frw mu cyumweru ku mucuruzi w' ibiribwa cyangwa ucuruza ibikoresho by' ibanze mu gihe aho SACCO ikorana n' amatsinda , buri tsinda ryari r@@ yemerewe kubikuza amafaranga yo kugabana ku buryo buri munyamuryango w' itsinda atar@@ enza ibihumbi 50 mu cyumweru .
Nyuma y' uko inama y' abaminisitiri yateranye kuwa 30 Mata 2020 yemereye bimwe mu bikorwa gukomeza , BNR yakuyeho ayo mabwiriza .
Itangazo ryashyizweho umukono na Guverineri wa BNR , John Rwangombwa rigira riti " Ib@@ ipimo ntarengwa byihariye byo kubikuza byari byashyizweho n' itangazo ryo kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 bik@@ uweho kugira ngo abanyamuryango b' ayo makoperative babashe gukora imirimo yabo nta nzitizi .
BNR yasabye SACCO gukomeza gukurikiza amategeko n' amabwiriza asanzwe agenga urwego rw' imari iciriritse .
Uko ikoranabuhanga ry@@ unguye bamwe rig@@ ah@@ ombya abandi kubera Coronavirus
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwand@@ urwa n' abarenga miliyoni enye kig@@ ahitana abasaga ibihumbi 28@@ 7 , ku Isi yose , kir@@ av@@ umirwa ku gahera n' abakora ibikorwa by' ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo by' ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kuby@@ inira ku ruk@@ oma .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus kimaze kwand@@ urwa n' abarenga miliyoni enye kig@@ ahitana abasaga ibihumbi 28@@ 7 , ku Isi yose , kir@@ av@@ umirwa ku gahera n' abakora ibikorwa by' ubucuruzi , nubwo bamwe mu bafite ibigo by' ikoranabuhanga bakomeje kuby@@ inira ku ruk@@ oma .
Bitewe n' ingamba zitandukanye zo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus , ibihugu bitandukanye byafashe cyane cyane gahunda ya ' guma mu rugo ' , abaturage benshi bar@@ ifashisha ikoranabuhanga mu gusaba serivisi , kugura no gutuma ibicuruzwa ndetse no kuganira no gukora inama .
Bitewe no gukorera mu rugo , ibigo bitanga serivisi z' ikoranabuhanga rifasha abantu kuganira no kuba bakora inama ari benshi byar@@ ungutse .
Urugero ni nka Z@@ oom ikomeje gufasha abantu benshi gukora inama .
Nubwo hari ibibazo by' umutekano byakomeje kuvugwa kuri Z@@ oom , ntibyabujije abay@@ ikoresha ndetse n' igiciro cyayo kwiyongera , aho cy@@ ikubye inshuro zirenga ebyiri kuva mu Ukuboza .
Umubare w' abakoresha Z@@ oom wavuye kuri miliyoni 10 ku munsi ugera kuri miliyoni 200 .
Ik@@ oreshwa mu nzego zose kuva ku bakora inama z' abaminisitiri kugeza ku bashumba bifuza kuvugana uko umukamo uhagaze n' ibindi .
Hari kandi abakoresha ubundi buryo .

Y@@ erekana ibiganiro byo mu bihugu bitandukanye biciye kuri internet birimo nka filime mbarankuru n' iz@@ ' ubundi bwoko , ariko bigasaba kubanza kuba umufat@@ abuguzi .

Y@@ abonye abay@@ ikoresha bashya bagera kuri miliyoni 16 muri ibi bihe bya Coronavirus .

Banki y' u Rwanda Itsura Amajyambere , BRD , yabaye iya mbere yo mu Rwanda igenz@@ uwe n' Ikigo Mpuzamahanga gik@@ urikirana ibijyanye n' imyenda n' Ubushakashatsi mu by' Imari , Fit@@ ch R@@ at@@ ings , iy@@ iha inota rya ' B + ' rigaragaza ko imari yayo ihagaze neza ndetse n' ahazaza h@@ ayo hameze neza .

Gahunda yo kuzahura ubukungu nyuma y' icyorezo cya Coronavirus igaragaza ko u Rwanda rushobora kuz@@ akoresha agera muri miliyari 88@@ 2 Frw mu myaka ibiri y' ingengo y' imari , ni ukuvuga uyu turimo wa 2019 / 20 n' utaha wa 2020 / 21 uzatangira muri Nyakanga .
Icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyatumye ibikorwa byinshi b@@ ifungwa , ndetse n' ubwo Guverinoma iheruka gufata umwanzuro ko bimwe b@@ ifungurwa nyuma y' iminsi isaga 40 , byasabwe gukoresha abakozi bake , kandi big@@ afungura hagati ya saa kumi n' imwe za mu gitondo na saa mbili z' ijoro .
Minisiteri y' Imari n' Igenamigambi yakoze gahunda igamije kuzahura ubukungu bw' u Rwanda , zirimo gushyigikira ibikorwa by' ubuvuzi , kwita ku batishoboye , gutera inkunga ibigo bya leta , inkunga ya leta mu kigega cyo kuzahura ubukungu n' izindi ngamba zigamije guhangana n' ingaruka za Coronavirus .
Bumwe mu buryo burimo kwifashisha mu korohereza ibigo byag@@ izweho ingaruka na Coronavirus , harimo uburyo bwo kuvanaho imwe mu misoro , aho kubara av@@ ansi y' umusoro ku nyungu z' ibigo n' iz@@ ' abantu ku giti cyabo , biz@@ ashingira ku by@@ acur@@ ujwe uyu mwaka .
Ibiny@@ abiziga bikora imirimo ibyara inyungu nabyo biz@@ ishyura av@@ ansi y' umusoro ku nyungu hashingiwe ku mubare w' amezi y' umwaka bizaba byar@@ akoz@@ emo iyo mirimo ibyara inyungu , ndetse udupfukamunwa duk@@ orerwa mu Rwanda nat@@ wo twas@@ on@@ ewe umusoro ku nyungu , mu rwego rwo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .

Ati " Hari imishinga y' imihanda , iy@@ ' amazi , iy@@ ' amashanyarazi , kugira ngo amafaranga agere ku bantu " " " " .

Indi gahunda yihariye igamije gufasha abashoramari n' abikorera mu byiciro bitandukanye bagizweho ingaruka n' iki cyorezo , aho leta yashyizeho gahunda yo gutangiza ikigega kiba@@ fasha kubona amafaranga yo gukoresha .

" Icyo kigega cyar@@ an@@ og@@ ejwe , harimo inkunga yihariye ku mahoteli kuko bigaragara ko ubukerarugendo biz@@ amara igihe kugira ngo bw@@ ongere buz@@ anz@@ amuk@@ e kuko ntibit@@ erwa n' uko ibihe byifashe mu Rwanda ahubwo uko byifashe ku Isi hose .

Yavuze ko icyo kigega " kizafasha ubucuruzi ubwo aribwo bwose bwag@@ izweho ingaruka , hari ibipimo biz@@ agend@@ erwaho kugira ngo aba@@ birimo babone amafaranga aciriritse ku gihe cyiza noneho bongere bakore bih@@ ut@@ ishe imirimo " " " " .

Iyi nkunga ni inguzanyo iciriritse izafasha Guverinoma y' u Rwanda kuvugurura ingengo y' imari hagamijwe kwitegura no guhangana n' ingaruka zatewe n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus mu rwego rw' ingufu .
Icyiciro cya gatatu cy' umushinga wo guteza imbere urwego rw' amashanyarazi , ni icya nyuma mu mushinga mugari wagombaga gutwara miliyoni 37@@ 5 z' amadolari , inguzanyo ya mbere yo gutangiza uwo mushinga ikaba yarat@@ anzwe mu Ukuboza 2017 , iya nyuma yatanzwe umwaka ushize .
Uwo mushinga ugomba kur@@ angirana na 2020 , ugamije gufasha mu iterambere ry' urwego rw' amashanyarazi mu Rwanda nkuko biri muri gahunda y' Igihugu y' Iterambere , NS@@ T@@ 1 , mu ntego yo kugeza amashanyarazi kuri bose bitarenze mu 2024 .
Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr .
Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko inkunga bahawe izafasha mu guharanira ko serivisi z' amashanyarazi zikomeza gutangwa nta kir@@ og@@ oya .
Yagize ati " Nubwo ingaruka za COVID - 19 byitezwe ko ziz@@ arangira , urwego rw' ingufu byitezwe ko ruz@@ ahura n' ibibazo nyamara gukomeza gutanga serivisi z' amashanyarazi bir@@ akenewe cyane kugira ngo serivisi rusange zikom@@ eze , big@@ abanye icyuho mu isubira inyuma ry' ubukungu kandi abatishoboye bakomeze kw@@ at@@ abwaho .
Umuyobozi wa Banki y' Isi , Ishami ry' u Rwanda , Yass@@ er El Gam@@ m@@ al , yavuze ko yizeye ko inkunga yatanzwe izafasha u Rwanda gusubira vuba mu murongo w' iterambere ry' ubukungu .
Ati " N@@ izeye ko kubera ubuyobozi bwiza , ukw@@ ihangana kw@@ ' Abanyarwanda , ingamba zafashwe na Guverinoma , inkunga ya Banki y' Isi n' abandi bafatanyabikorwa mu iterambere izafasha u Rwanda kwig@@ obotora iki cyorezo rus@@ ubire mu nzira nziza .
Mu mpera z' uyu mushinga mu Ukuboza 2020 byitezwe ko ingo 61 % mu Rwanda zizaba zig@@ erwaho n' amashanyarazi , bit@@ ange icyizere ku kugera ku 100 % mu mwaka wa 2024 .
Uyu mushinga kandi kunoza imicungire y' amashanyarazi hag@@ abanywa ingano it@@ akara , kugabanya igiciro no kongera umusaruro w' ikigo kiy@@ acuruza n' ibindi .

Gutwara amafi yo muri Tanzania akag@@ ezwa mu Burayi , ni amahirwe ku bar@@ obyi n' abacuruzi b' amafi bo muri icyo gihugu bari bamaze igihe bifuza uburyo bub@@ oroh@@ ereye bwo kugeza umusaruro wabo ku masoko yo mu mahanga , bakag@@ orwa n' igiciro cy' urugendo .
Ubusanzwe abacuruzi b' amafi bajyaga babanza kugeza umusaruro wabo ku bibuga by' indege bya Entebbe muri Uganda na Nairobi muri Kenya , kugira ngo indege ziw@@ ugeze ku masoko yo hanze , ibintu bavuga ko by@@ abah@@ endaga .

Uko umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda w@@ iyongereyeho miliyari zirenga 3@@ 000Frw mu myaka itanu
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe n' Isi yose bih@@ anganye n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bw@@ ubak@@ iyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi n' ibindi bit@@ ah@@ wemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rw@@ abyo mu musaruro mbumbe w' igihugu ruk@@ igaragaza .
Nubwo u Rwanda kimwe n' Isi yose bih@@ anganye n' icyorezo cya Coronavirus , mbere yacyo ubukungu bwarwo bwakomeje kwiyongera mu nkingi zose bw@@ ubak@@ iyeho , aho ubuhinzi , inganda , serivisi n' ibindi bit@@ ah@@ wemye kuzamuka umwaka ku wundi kandi uruhare rw@@ abyo mu musaruro mbumbe w' igihugu ruk@@ igaragaza .
Imibare Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' Ibarurishamibare ( NIS@@ R ) , cyatangaje kuwa 24 Werurwe 2020 , igaragaza ko mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda ( G@@ D@@ P ) , wiyongereye ku rugero rwa 9 .
4 % , ugera kuri miliyari 9@@ 105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8@@ 18@@ 9 Frw war@@ iho mu 2018 .
Muri uyu musaruro mbumbe , ubuhinzi bwagize uruhare rwa 24 % inganda zigira uruhare rwa 18 % , Serivisi zingana 49 % mu gihe ibindi bisigaye byagize uruhare ku kigero cya 9 % .
Iri z@@ amuka ry' ubukungu rir@@ atanga icyizere ko nta gihindutse ibyo u Rwanda rut@@ eganya ko nibura mu 20@@ 35 ruzaba rufite ubukungu buciriritse bishoboka .
Icyo gihe birasaba ko ubukungu bwaba bwih@@ uta ku 10 % , bigatuma umunyarwanda yaz@@ aba yinjiza asaga miliyoni 10 Frw ku mwaka .
Rir@@ ashimangira kandi imbaraga leta y' u Rwanda ikomeje gushyira mu guteza imbere ubukungu .
Mu 1994 , izamuka ry' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda , r@@ yasubiye inyuma kuri - 41 .
9 % , umusaruro mbumbe w' umuturage wari amadolari 14@@ 6 ku mwaka .
Nubwo inzira ikiri ndende , aho iterambere ry' ubukungu bw' u Rwanda rigeze har@@ ivugira kuko nko mu myaka itanu ishize umusaruro mbumbe wavuye kuri miliyari miliyari 5 9@@ 56 Frw mu 2015 , ugera kuri miliyari 9@@ 105 Frw .
Us@@ ubije amaso inyuma , usanga umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda mu myaka itanu ishize ( 2015 - 2019 ) , war@@ iyongereyeho miliyari 3@@ 14@@ 9 Frw .
Iri z@@ amuka rishingiye ahanini kuri gahunda yo guteza imbere ubuhinzi , ishoramari muri serivisi zitandukanye , ubucuruzi , inganda n' ibindi bic@@ umbi by' ubukungu .
Iz@@ amuka ry' umusaruro mbumbe mu myaka itanu
Mu 2015 umusaruro mbumbe w' u Rwanda w@@ azamutseho 6 .
9 % , aho wang@@ anaga na miliyari 5 9@@ 56 Frw zikaba zari zivuye kuri miliyari 4 9@@ 15@@ Frw mu 2014 .
Mu 2016 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 6 , 6@@ 18 Frw , aho wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 .
9 % ugereranyije n' umwaka wabanje .
Mu 2017 umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 7 59@@ 7 ukaba war@@ azamutse 6 .
1 % , mu 2018 wageze kuri miliyari 8@@ 18@@ 9 Frw uz@@ amutse ku kigero cya 8 .
6 % ugereranyije n' umwaka wabanje wa 2017 .
Ubwo hatangazwa umusaruro mbumbe wa 2018 , Minisitiri w' Imari n' Igenamigambi , Dr Uzziel Ndagijimana , yavuze ko iterambere ry' ubuhinzi , inganda , ibikorerwa mu Rwanda na serivisi by@@ azamuye ubukungu cyane .
Yagize ati " Ngira ngo muzi gahunda ya Made in Rwanda no korohereza ibikorwa bikorerwa mu Rwanda , biragenda rero bitanga umusaruro , umusaruro w' inganda ur@@ azamuka cyane " " " " .
Minisitiri Ndagijimana yavuze ko mu bitanga umusaruro harimo ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi byaba imihanda n' inganda .
Icyo gihe ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi byazamutseho 20 % , mu nganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye cy@@ azamutseho kuri 13 % , umusaruro w' inganda zitunganya ibiryo ni 10 % , iz@@ itunganya imyenda ni 26 % na 38 % ku musaruro w' inganda zikora ibikoresho bikoze mu byuma .
Mu 2019 , umusaruro mbumbe wageze kuri miliyari 9@@ 105 Frw uvuye kuri miliyari 8@@ 18@@ 9 Frw war@@ iho mu 2018 .
Bis@@ obanuye ko hiyongereyeho miliyoni 9@@ 16@@ Frw mu mwaka umwe .
Urwego rwa serivisi rw@@ ashinze imizi
Mu 2015 , urwego rwa serivisi rw@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 7 % rugira uruhare mu musaruro mbumbe wose rwa 47 % .
Mu 2016 serivisi z@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 6 % .
Muri uwo mwaka serivisi zishingiye kuri hoteli na restaurant z@@ azamutse ku rugero rwa 11 % bitewe na gahunda yo kwakira inama n' ibikorwa bitandukanye .
Imirimo y' ubwikorezi yazamutse ku rugero rwa 8 % ahanini bitewe n' ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bw@@ azamutse ku rugero rwa 15 % .
Mu 2017 , serivisi z@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho uruhare rw@@ azo mu musaruro mbumbe rugera kuri 46 % .
Mu 2018 umusaruro wa serivisi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 9 % naho mu 2019 uzamuka ku rugero rwa 8 % ndetse zigira uruhare rwa 49 % muri G@@ D@@ P .
Mu 2016 , uwari Minisitiri w' imari n' igenamigambi , Claver Gatete yavuze ko gahunda ya leta ijyanye no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga yagize uruhare runini mu kuzamura umusaruro mbumbe w' igihugu nk' aho ibijyanye na hotel na restaurant z@@ abigizemo uruhare runini .
Guhera muri Nyakanga 2018 kugeza Gashyantare 2019 , u Rwanda rwari rumaze kwinjiza miliyoni 52 z' amadolari ( asaga miliyari 46 Frw ) avuye mu gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga .
Mu mwaka w' ingengo y' imari ushize ( 2018 / 2019 ) igihugu cyari cy@@ ihaye intego yo kwinjiza miliyoni 74 z' amadolari mu bikorwa byo gutegura no kwakira inama mpuzamahanga , avuye kuri miliyoni 42 z@@ injijwe mu 2017 .
Kugeza ubu muri Kigali hari ibyumba bya hoteli z' inyenyeri ebyiri kugeza kuri eshanu bisaga 5000 , w@@ ashyiramo ibindi byumba by' inzu zigezweho zishobora gucumbikira abantu Kigali ifite bikagera ku 10 000 .
Ubucuruzi bud@@ and@@ aza n' ubug@@ urisha ibintu icyarimwe bw' ib@@ yakorewe mu Rwanda bukomeje kongera umusaruro wa serivisi , aho mu 2019 bw@@ iyongereye ku kigero cya 16 % .
Ubw@@ ikorezi bw@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 12 % ahanini bitewe n' ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere bw@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 17 % .
Serivisi z' imari z@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 8 % naho serivisi za hoteli na za restaurant ziz@@ amuka ku gipimo cya 10 % .
Inganda z@@ ifatiye runini ubukungu
Kuva mu 2015 , urwego rw' inganda rwagize ingufu nyinshi cyane mu bukungu bw' igihugu kuko ari bwo gahunda ya Made in Rwanda , yatangiraga gushyirwa mu bikorwa mu buryo buhamye .
Icyo gihe umusaruro w' inganda wazamutse ku kigero cya 7 % .
Muri buri turere kandi hashyizweho iby@@ anya byihariye by' inganda , ndetse no mu Mujyi wa Kigali , iki cy@@ anya gishyirwa i Masoro mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Mu 2016 inganda z@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 7 % , gahunda ya Made in Rwanda igira uruhare rukomeye cyane kuko inganda zikora imyenda , inkweto n' ibindi bituruka ku ruhu by@@ iyongereye ku rugero rwa 10 % , iz@@ ikora ibyo kurya ziyongera ku rugero rwa 8 % , naho inganda zikora ibikoresho by' ubwubatsi harimo is@@ ima z@@ iyongeraho 21 % .
Mu 2017 inganda z@@ azamutse ku kigero cya 4 % , mu 2018 ziz@@ amuka ku 10 % naho mu 2019 umusaruro uzamuka kuri 16 % .
Mu 2019 , izamuka ry' umusaruro w' inganda ryatewe ahanini n' ibikorwa by' ubwubatsi , inganda zitunganya ibintu bitandukanye n' ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro .
Kuri ubu mu Rwanda h@@ abarirwa inganda nto n' iz@@ iciriritse zirenga 800 zirimo inganda zitari zisanzwe mu Rwanda nk' iz@@ ikora telefoni , iz@@ iter@@ anya imodoka , iz@@ ikora ibiribwa n' izindi .
Ubuhinzi bukomeje gutera imbere
Imibare ya NIS@@ R , yerekana ko mu 2015 , ubuhinzi bw@@ azamutseho 5 % , ndetse bugira uruhare rwa 33 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Mu 2018 , umusaruro w' ubuhinzi wazamutse ku rugero rwa 6 % , mu 2019 , wazamutse ku kigero cya 5 % , naho umusaruro wabwo ugira uruhare rwa 24 % mu musaruro mbumbe .
Ubuhinzi nka kimwe mu bit@@ unze abanyarwanda benshi , bw@@ akunze guhura n' imbogamizi zirimo kuba bushingiye ku mvura , yabon@@ eka buk@@ agenda neza yabura buk@@ agenda nabi .
Ibi byatumye leta ishyira imbaraga muri gahunda yo kuhira aho kugeza ubu hegitari zirenga ibihumbi 68 z@@ uh@@ irwa .
Gukoresha inyongeramusaruro , guhuza ubutaka no guhinga igihingwa cy@@ atoranyijwe byit@@ aweho cyane .
Leta y' u Rwanda kandi yashyize imbere no gushyiraho inganda z@@ ongerera agaciro umusaruro ukomoka ku buhinzi n' ubworozi .
Umuyobozi wa NIS@@ R , Yusuf Murangwa avuga ko ' uyu mwaka wagenze neza kuruta uko byari byitezwe ' .
Ati " Ubuhinzi nabwo ntabwo bwakoze nabi 5 % nubwo haba h@@ ifuzwa ko biba byiza kurushaho " " " " .
Mu 2019 , ibihingwa ng@@ andur@@ arug@@ o by@@ iyongereye ku kigero cya 4 % , ibihingwa byoherezwa mu mahanga byiyongera 5 % bitewe n' ikawa yiyongereye ku kigero cya 7 % n' icyayi cy@@ iyongereye ku kigero cya 3 % .
Kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , ubukungu ku Isi hose buz@@ agabanuka , ubw@@ ' u Rwanda byitezwe ko buz@@ azamuka ku gipimo cya 2 % mu mwaka wa 2020 b@@ uvuye kuri 9 .
4 % bw@@ azamutseho umwaka ushize .
Icyakora kubera ingamba zafashwe mu kuzahura ubukungu , biteganyijwe ko ubukungu bw' u Rwanda mu mwaka wa 2021 buz@@ azamuka ku gipimo cya 6 .
3 % na 8 % mu 2022 .

Umwuka w' intambara ukomeje gut@@ utumba hagati ya Amerika na Iran
Nyuma y' igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kig@@ ahitana Gen Q@@ as@@ em Sol@@ eim@@ ani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe w' ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge n' ubwoba bw' intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse n' abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Nyuma y' igitero cyagabwe na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu rukerera rwo kuri uyu wa Gatanu , kig@@ ahitana Gen Q@@ as@@ em Sol@@ eim@@ ani , wari usanzwe ayobora umutwe udasanzwe w' ingabo zirinda abategetsi bakomeye muri Iran ; impungenge n' ubwoba bw' intambara bikomeje kwiyongera ku batari bake bakurikiranira hafi politiki ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , ndetse n' abatuye mu burasirazuba bwo hagati .
Iki gitero cy@@ ategetswe na Perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , Donald Trump , cyan@@ ah@@ itanye Abu Mah@@ di al - Muh@@ and@@ is , wari umuyobozi wungirije w' umutwe bivugwa ko ufash@@ wa na Iran witwa ( Popul@@ ar Mob@@ il@@ iz@@ ation Forces ) , ibiro by' ubutasi bya Amerika ( CIA ) byem@@ eje ko ariwo wateguye uk@@ anag@@ aba igitero kuri Ambasade ya Amerika mu mujyi wa Bag@@ d@@ ad mu minsi ishize .
Gen Q@@ as@@ em Sol@@ eim@@ ani na Abu Mah@@ di al - Muh@@ and@@ is baras@@ iwe ku kibuga cy' indege cya Iraq i Bag@@ d@@ ad , bari mu modoka hamwe n' abandi bantu batanu .
Umuyobozi w' ikirenga muri Iran , A@@ yat@@ ol@@ lah Ali K@@ ham@@ ene@@ i , wahise ategeka iminsi itatu y' icyunamo mu gihugu hose , yavuze ko hateganyijwe kwihorera gukomeye ku bishe Gen Q@@ as@@ em Sol@@ eim@@ ani .

Ati " Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ziz@@ irengera ingaruka z' ubujiji bwazo .

Ubuh@@ angange bwe kandi bwar@@ eb@@ erwaga mu ishusho y' uko yafatwaga nka nomero ya kabiri mu bafata ibyemezo muri Iran .

Leta y' u Buhinde iherutse gushyiraho itegeko ryemerera ubwenegihugu abaturage bava mu bihugu bituranye na bwo , bo mu madini yose usibye abo mu idini ya Islam .
Leta y' u Buhinde iherutse gushyiraho itegeko ryemerera ubwenegihugu abaturage bava mu bihugu bituranye na bwo , bo mu madini yose usibye abo mu idini ya Islam .
Impuguke mu mategeko zo zivuga ko iri tegeko rih@@ abanye cyane n' itegeko Nshinga ry' iki gihugu , riteganya ko amadini yose angana imbere y' amategeko .
Iri tegeko rishya rigenga uburyo bwo kubona ubwenegihugu mu Buhinde , rije nyuma yo kuvugurura ir@@ yari risanzwe ryo mu mwaka w' 195@@ 5 , r@@ yem@@ ereraga ba nyamuk@@ e bafat@@ waga nabi bo mu madini y' aba - H@@ ind@@ us , S@@ ik@@ h@@ s , Bud@@ d@@ h@@ ist@@ s , J@@ ain@@ s , Par@@ s@@ is , n' abakirisitu bava mu bihugu nka Banglad@@ esh , Afghanistan na Pakistan , ariko ntir@@ igire icyo rivuga ku bay@@ isilamu .
Iri tegeko r@@ yageze mu nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Buhinde bigizwemo uruhare cyane n' ishyaka riri ku butegetsi ry' aba - H@@ indu [ B@@ har@@ atiya Jan@@ ata Party ] , r@@ yemejwe na perezida w' iki gihugu R@@ am Nat@@ h K@@ ov@@ in@@ d , tariki ya 12 Ukuboza , 2019 .
Amashyaka atavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi avuga ko iri tegeko rishya ririmo ivangura , kuko rir@@ obanura idini ya Islam mu gihugu gituwe n' abasaga miliyari 1 .
3 bizwi neza ko gitanga ubwisanzure ku madini yose .
Aba - Islam bo mu Buhinde bangana hafi na 15 % by' abaturage bose .
Aban@@ enga iri tegeko bavuga ko byakozwe mu mugambi w' igihe kirekire wa Guverinoma iyobowe na Minisitiri w' intebe Nar@@ end@@ ra Mod@@ i , kuva yajya ku butegetsi mu myaka itandatu ishize .

Ati " Politiki ya ' B@@ J@@ P ' ni uguh@@ oza u Buhinde mu mwuka mubi no kuzamura uburakari bw' abaturage cyane cyane mu gihe cy' amatora .

Perezida : Pasteur Bizimungu
Pasteur Bizimungu ni we wahise agirwa Perezida w' inzibacyuho .
Uyu mugabo uvuka muri Gisenyi , yari umunyamuryango wa FPR Inkotanyi wigeze no kuyobora ikigo cya Elect@@ rog@@ az cyahoze gishinzwe ingufu ku butegetsi bwa Perezida Juvenal Habyarimana .

Mu 2006 Bizimungu yandikiye ibaruwa Perezida Kagame asaba imbabazi , az@@ ihabwa mu 2007 ahita arekurwa .

Paul Kagame yagumye kuri uwo mwanya kugeza muri Werurwe 2000 ubwo yat@@ orer@@ waga gusimbura Bizimungu ku mwanya wa Perezida .
Ni inshingano yakoze neza ndetse aza gutorerwa izindi manda , kugeza uyu munsi .
Minisitiri w' Intebe : Faustin Twagiramungu
Guverinoma ya mbere yag@@ iyeho nyuma ya Jenoside yari iyobowe na Faustin Twagiramungu nka Minisitiri w' Intebe .
Twagiramungu w' ishyaka MDR ni umwe mu banye@@ politiki bari barah@@ anganye n' ingoma ya Habyarimana , bashyigikiye imigambi y' ubumwe n' ubwiyunge mu banyarwanda .
Uyu mugabo uvuka mu yahoze ari perefegitura ya Cyangugu , yaje kwegura tariki 28 Kanama 1995 , ahita afata iy@@ ' ubuhungiro agana mu B@@ ubul@@ igi ari naho ak@@ iba .
As@@ igaye agaragara mu bikorwa birwanya Leta y' u Rwanda ndetse aherutse kwifatanya n' Ihuriro P5 ry' amashyaka aba hanze y' u Rwanda , atavuga rumwe na Guverinoma y' u Rwanda .
Minisitiri w' Intebe wungirije & Minisitiri w' umurimo : Alexis Kanyar@@ engwe
Kanyar@@ engwe Alexis wo mu Muryango FPR Inkotanyi ni we wahawe umwanya wa Minisitiri w' umurimo akaba na Minisitiri w' Intebe wungirije .
Uyu mugabo ukomoka mu yahoze ari Ruhengeri ( Amajyaruguru ) , ni umwe mu bahoze ari ibikom@@ erezwa ku ngoma ya Habyarimana dore ko ari umwe mu basirikare 11 bafatanyije na Habyarimana guhirika ubutegetsi bwa Gr√©g@@ oire Kayibanda kuwa 5 Nyakanga 1973 .
Kanyar@@ engwe wafat@@ waga nka nimero ya kabiri ku butegetsi bwa Habyarimana , baje gushwana mu 1980 ashinjwa gushaka kumuh@@ irika , nyuma aza guhunga igihugu ari nabwo yifat@@ anyaga na FPR mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu .
Kanyar@@ engwe wabaye umuyobozi w' Umuryango FPR Inkotanyi kugeza mu 1998 , yaje kuvanwa muri Guverinoma mu 1997 .
Alexis Kanyar@@ engwe yitabye Imana tariki 13 Ugushyingo 2006 azize uburwayi , ashyingurwa mu irimbi rya Remera mu mujyi wa Kigali .
Minisitiri w' ububanyi n' amahanga : Jean Marie Ndagijimana
Nk@@ ' igihugu cyari kimaze kuva muri Jenoside , ibihugu byinshi big@@ ifata nk' ik@@ itar@@ iho , ntabwo by@@ ashobokaga kwisubiza ikuzo hatabayeho kugira Minisiteri y' ububanyi n' amahanga kandi ikora cyane .
Ndagijimana wari mu ishyaka MDR ni we wahawe uwo mwanya at@@ amaz@@ eho kabiri .
Uyu mugabo uvuka mu yahoze ari Cyangugu yamaze amezi ane kuri uwo mwanya , aza guhungira mu Bufaransa atwaye amafaranga yari yahawe ngo ajye gufung@@ uza za ambasade .
Perezida Paul Kagame aherutse kub@@ ikom@@ ozaho ati " Minisitiri w' ububanyi n' amahanga wa mbere wag@@ iyeho icyo gihe yag@@ ambanye n' abandi bayobozi muri Guverinoma nka Minisitiri w' Intebe icyo gihe , ahabwa amafaranga mu ntoki , ibihumbi amagana by' amadolari , ngo ajye mu mahanga as@@ ubuk@@ ure ibikorwa bya za ambasade cyangwa afung@@ uze insh@@ ya .
Uyu mugabo ntabwo yagarutse !
Kandi yari amaze amezi angahe mu kazi , iyo yari guverinoma ya mbere y' inzibacyuho .
Minisitiri w' Umutekano : S@@ eth Send@@ ash@@ onga
Guverinoma y' inzibacyuho yashyizwe kuwa 19 Nyakanga 1994 , ntiy@@ asize n' umwanya wa Minisitiri w' Umutekano .
Uwo mwanya wahawe S@@ eth Send@@ ash@@ onga w@@ akomokaga mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Kibuye , wari impunzi muri Kenya ku butegetsi bwa Perezida Habyarimana .
Send@@ ash@@ onga wari umunyamuryango wa FPR Inkotanyi , yavuye muri Guverinoma mu 1995 ahita ajya mu buhungiro muri Kenya .
Aho niho yaje kuras@@ irwa tariki 16 Gicurasi 1998 .
Perezida Paul Kagame aherutse kuvuga ko Send@@ ash@@ onga nyuma yo guhunga igihugu yakoranye n' abash@@ akaga guhungabanya umutekano ku buryo yari yatangiye ' kurenga umurongo ' .
Minisitiri w' Ubutabera : Alphonse Marie Nkubito
Minisiteri y' ubutabera yahawe umunya - Cyangugu , Alphonse Marie Nkubito wari impirimbanyi y' uburenganzira bwa muntu .
Nkubito yayoboye iyo Minisiteri kugeza mu 1995 .
Yaje kwitaba Imana kuwa 13 Gashyantare 1996 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri w' Uburezi : Pierre - C√©lestin RW@@ IG@@ EMA
Pierre - C√©lestin Rwigema uvuka i Gitarama mu Ntara y' Amajyepfo ubu , ni we wagizwe Minisitiri wa mbere w' Uburezi bw' amashuri abanza n' ayisumbuye nyuma ya Jenoside .
Rwigema wari mu ishyaka MDR , yaje kuva kuri uwo mwanya aba Minisitiri w' Intebe asimbuye Faustin Twagiramungu .
Umwanya wa Minisitiri w' Intebe yaw@@ uv@@ uyeho muri Werurwe 2000 , aza guhungira muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Yagarutse mu gihugu mu mwaka wa 2011 , aza no gutorerwa kuba umudepite uhagarariye u Rwanda mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' Umuryango wa Afurika y' Iburasirazuba ( EALA ) ari nawo akiriho kugeza ubu .
Minisitiri w' Amashuri Makuru n' ubushakashatsi : Dr Joseph Nsengimana
Dr Nsengimana ni we wagizwe Minisitiri w' amashuri makuru n' ubushakashatsi .
Uyu mugabo wavukiye i Busogo muri Musanze yashyizwe kuri uyu mwanya kubera ko yari asanzwe ari inzobere mu bijyanye n' uburezi , dore ko yabaye umwarimu muri Kaminuza zirimo iy@@ ' u Rwanda n' iya Lubum@@ ba@@ shi .
Nyuma yahawe indi myanya ikomeye irimo kuba minisitiri w' abakozi ba Leta n' umurimo , Minisitiri w' ubutaka , gutuza abantu no kurengera ibidukikije ndetse aba umujyanama wihariye wa Perezida Paul Kagame .
Guhera mu 2006 yagiye mu kazi ko kuba ambasaderi , agas@@ oza mu 2014 ubwo yari ahagarariye u Rwanda muri Ethiopia no mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe .
Ubu Nsengimana aba mu Rwanda aho akorera imirimo itandukanye .
Minisitiri w' Imari : Marc Rug@@ enera
Ibig@@ ega n' isanduku by' igihugu muri Guverinoma ya mbere byarag@@ ijwe Marc Rug@@ enera , umunya - Gitarama wo mu ishyaka PSD .
Uwo mwanya Rug@@ enera yaw@@ uv@@ uyeho mu 1997 aba Minisitiri w' Ubucuruzi nyuma aba Minisitiri w' ubukerarugendo .
Ubu Rug@@ enera yashinze ndetse ayobora ikigo cy' ubwishingizi cya Radi@@ ant .
Minisitiri w' Inganda : Prosper Higiro
Minisitiri w' inganda wa mbere nyuma ya Jenoside yabaye Prosper Higiro , umur@@ wanashyaka wa PL ukomoka mu yahoze ari Kibungo .
Uyu mugabo w' imyaka 58 , nyuma yo kuva muri Guverinoma yabaye umus@@ enateri ndetse n' umwe mu bakandida biy@@ amamaje ku mwanya wa Perezida wa Repubulika mu matora yo mu 2010 .
Higiro aherutse kugirwa ambasaderi muri Canada .
Uyu yabaye umuyobozi mu nzego zitandukanye zirimo kuba Umunyamabanga Mukuru w' Ihuriro ry' Inteko z@@ ishinga Amategeko z' Umuryango uhuza ibihugu byo mu Karere k' Ibiyaga Big@@ ari ( F@@ P - IC@@ G@@ R@@ L ) .
Minisitiri w' Ubuzima : Dr Joseph Karemera
Karemera wahoze ari impunzi muri Uganda , ni umunyarwanda ukomoka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Byumba , wabaye Minisitiri wa mbere w' ubuzima w' u Rwanda rwa nyuma ya Jenoside .
Uwo mwanya yaw@@ uv@@ uyeho agirwa Minisitiri w' Uburezi .
Ntak@@ ivugwa cyane ariko ni umwe mu bag@@ itanga ibitekerezo bih@@ amye mu muryango wa politiki akomokamo ari wo FPR Inkotanyi .
Minisitiri ushinzwe itumanaho no gutwara abantu n' ibintu : Immacul√©e Gahima Kayumba
Gahima wo mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi , ni umunya - Butare wabaye mu buhungiro mu gihugu cy' u Burundi mbere ya Jenoside .
Nubwo atak@@ ivugwa cyane , Madamu Gahima wan@@ abaye umus@@ enateri ubu ari mu Rwanda aho akorera imirimo itandukanye .
Minisitiri w' imibereho myiza : Mugabo P@@ ie
Mugabo P@@ ie yabaye Minisitiri w' imibereho myiza y' abaturage muri Guverinoma ya mbere y' ubumwe , ari umuyoboke w' ishyaka PL .
Uyu mugabo w' inzobere mu mategeko yanabaye umucamanza na Perezida w' Urukiko rukuru .
Aba mu Rwanda aho atanga serivisi zitandukanye zijyanye n' iby@@ ' amategeko .
Minisitiri ushinzwe impunzi : Dr Jacques Bihoz@@ agara
Nk@@ ' igihugu cyari kivuye muri Jenoside n' intambara yo kubohora igihugu , hari abaturage basaga miliyoni ebyiri bahunze kandi bak@@ enewe mu kongera kubaka igihugu .
Byari ngombwa gushyiraho Minisiteri ishinzwe gucyura impunzi , cyane ko ubuhunzi bwari mu bibazo byatumye FPR Inkotanyi ishingwa .
Dr Bihoz@@ agara yitabye Imana muri Werurwe 2016 , agwa muri Gereza ya Mp@@ imba mu Burundi aho yari amaze umwaka afungiwe kubera impamvu za politiki .
Minisitiri w' Umuryango n' Iterambere ry' umugore : Iny@@ umba Aloy@@ sia
Iny@@ umba w@@ akomokaga mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi ni we wagizwe Minisitiri ushinzwe iterambere ry' umuryango n' umugore .
Nk@@ ' uwat@@ urukaga mu muryango FPR Inkotanyi , Iny@@ umba yatangije urugamba rwo gut@@ inyura no gushishikariza abagore kumva ko bashoboye , nyuma y' uko bari bamaze no kugira uruhare mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu .
Y@@ itabye Imana tariki 6 Ukuboza 2012 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri w' Urubyiruko n' amashyirahamwe : Patrick Maz@@ im@@ h@@ aka
Uyu mugabo wabaye umuyobozi wungirije wa FPR Inkotanyi mbere gato y' urugamba rwo guhagarika Jenoside , ni we wahawe kuyobora urubyiruko muri Guverinoma ya mbere yabayeho nyuma ya Jenoside .
Muri 2003 yatorewe kuba umuyobozi wungirije muri Komisiyo y' Akanama ka Afurika yunze Ubumwe .
Y@@ itabye Imana ku wa 25 Mutarama 2018 azize uburwayi .
Minisitiri w' ingufu n' imirimo rusange : Charles Ntakirut@@ inka
Charles Ntakirut@@ inka yabaye Minisitiri w' ingufu n' imirimo rusange nk' umunyamuryango w' ishyaka PSD .
Ntakirut@@ inka uvuka ku Gikongoro , mu 2001 afatanyije na Pasteur Bizimungu wahoze ari Perezida bashinze ishyaka P@@ DR Ubuy@@ anja ritari r@@ yemewe n' amategeko .
Yat@@ awe muri yombi mu gihe kimwe na Bizimungu mu 2002 , aham@@ y@@ wa ibyaha birimo gukangurira abaturage kwig@@ umura no kurema umutwe w' abagizi ba nabi .
Yak@@ atiwe igifungo cy' imyaka icumi , ayir@@ angiza mu 2012 .
Ubu yasubiye mu buzima busanzwe ariko ntak@@ igaragara mu bikorwa bya Politiki .
Minisitiri w' ubukerarugendo n' ibidukikije : Nay@@ inzira Jean - N@@ √©p@@ om@@ usc@@ √®ne
Nay@@ inzira yabaye Minisitiri w' Ibidukikije n' ubukerarugendo muri guverinoma yaguye y' inzibacyuho yatangajwe ku wa 19 Nyakanga 1994 , yari iyobowe na Faustin Twagiramungu .
Yaje kuba umudepite ariko mu 2002 aza kwegura mu nteko ishinga Amategeko ashinjwa imyitwarire idahwitse .
Nay@@ inzira yagarutse mu ruhando rwa politiki ahatanira kuba Perezida wa Repubulika nk' umukandida wigenga , mu matora ya Perezida yo mu 2003 .
Uyu mugabo wavukiye mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Gisenyi ku wa 10 Werurwe 194@@ 3 , yitabye Imana kuwa 13 Kanama 2014 .
Minisitiri w' Ubuhinzi , Ubw@@ orozi n' Amash@@ yamba : Dr Iyamuremye Augustin
Iyamuremye wo mu ishyaka PSD ni we wabaye Minisitiri Minisitiri w' Ubuhinzi , Ubw@@ orozi n' amashyamba muri Guverinoma ya mbere y' Ubumwe , icyakora we yashyizweho tariki 18 Kanama 1994 hashize ukwezi abandi bari mu mirimo .
Yabaye Minisitiri w' Ububanyi n' Amahanga kuva mu 1999 kugeza muri 2000 .
Yan@@ abaye kandi Minisitiri w' Itangazamakuru .
Iyamuremye ni we wayoboye Komisiyo yashinzwe kwiga ku ngingo z' Itegeko Nshinga ryavuguruwe mu 2015 .
Kuri ubu Iyamuremye ni umuyobozi w' Urwego rw' Igihugu Ng@@ ishwanama rw' In@@ araribonye .
Minisitiri w' Igenamigambi , Bir@@ ara Jean - Ber@@ ch@@ mas
Bir@@ ara yagizwe Minisitiri tariki 2 Nzeri 1994 nyuma y' amezi asaga abiri Guverinoma nshya ig@@ iyeho .
Ni umuny@@ apol@@ iti uvuka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Gisenyi .
Y@@ iruk@@ anywe muri Guverinoma mu Ukwakira 1997 .
Ubu ari mu kiruhuko cy' izabukuru , aba mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Minisitiri w' Itangazamakuru : N@@ kul@@ iy@@ ingoma Jean Baptiste
N@@ kul@@ iy@@ ingoma yagizwe Minisitiri ahagarariye ishyaka MDR .
Ak@@ om@@ oka mu yahoze ari Perefegitura ya Byumba .
Y@@ avuye muri Guverinoma muri Kanama 1995 ubwo Twagiramungu wari Minisitiri w' Intebe yeg@@ uraga , bombi bafata iy@@ ' ubuhungiro .
Urebye urutonde rw' abaminisitiri ba Guverinoma ya mbere yag@@ iyeho nyuma ya Jenoside , nta n' umwe ukiri muri Guverinoma .
B@@ ake baracyari mu mirimo ya leta , abandi bari mu kiruhuko cy' izabukuru kubera imyaka bagezeho ; bahunze igihugu kubera amakosa bakoze abandi bakomeje imirimo mu rwego rw' abikorera .
RDC : Umudepite yasubije Muz@@ ito wasabye ko u Rwanda rw@@ om@@ ekwa kuri Congo ngo ibone amahoro
Umudepite akaba n' Umuyobozi w' ishyaka En@@ v@@ ol muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Del@@ ly S@@ es@@ anga , yamaganye igitekerezo cy' umunyapolitiki Adolphe Muz@@ ito uherutse gusaba ko igihugu cye gitera u Rwanda rukom@@ ekwa kuri RDC kugira ngo amahoro abon@@ eke mu Burasirazuba .
Umudepite akaba n' Umuyobozi w' ishyaka En@@ v@@ ol muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , Del@@ ly S@@ es@@ anga , yamaganye igitekerezo cy' umunyapolitiki Adolphe Muz@@ ito uherutse gusaba ko igihugu cye gitera u Rwanda rukom@@ ekwa kuri RDC kugira ngo amahoro abon@@ eke mu Burasirazuba .
Amagambo ya Muz@@ ito uvugira ihuriro ry' amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Leta , L@@ amuka , ku ikubitiro yamag@@ aniwe kure na bamwe mu bayobozi bakomeye muri iryo huriro barimo Moise Katumbi na Jean Pierre Bemba .
Kuri uyu wa Gatandatu ubwo yari yahuye n' abarwanashyaka b' ishaka rye b@@ ifur@@ izanya umwaka mushya , Del@@ ly S@@ es@@ anga , yabajijwe niba na we abona amahoro mu Burasirazuba bwa Congo az@@ aturuka mu gutera u Rwanda bakar@@ wiy@@ om@@ ekaho .
Umuyobozi wa En@@ v@@ ol akaba n' Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Congo , S@@ es@@ anga yamaganye amagambo ya Muz@@ ito , avuga ko amahoro ya Congo az@@ aturuka imbere muri Congo .
Yagize ati " Intambara sicyo gisubizo .
Iyi ntambara ahubwo yak@@ arw@@ anywe hagamijwe kuzana ubumwe imbere mu gihugu , gukuraho imikorere mibi y' ubuyobozi , ruswa , ikimeny@@ ane byaz@@ ang@@ ereje leta bikan@@ agira ingaruka ku nzego z' umutekano .
S@@ es@@ anga yavuze ko igisirikare cya Congo kitab@@ uze imbaraga zo gutsinda intambara ziri mu Burasirazuba nk' uko bamwe babik@@ ega , ahubwo ngo ni imikorere mibi .
Ati " Ab@@ anye - Congo bazi kurwana , baraby@@ er@@ akanye mu Ntambara ya Mbere n' iya Kabiri z' isi yose .
Yavuze ko imbaraga nyinshi zikwiriye gushyirwa mu kurwanya ibibazo byugarije igihugu biri imbere kurusha kwitwaza ibyo hanze , nk' uko ikinyamakuru Polit@@ ico cyab@@ itangaje .
Mbere yo kuba umudepite , S@@ es@@ anga yakoze mu myanya itandukanye muri Congo harimo no kuba Minisitiri w' igenamigambi .
Musenyeri wa Kinshasa , Fr@@ id@@ ol@@ in Amb@@ ongo , na we aherutse kuvuga ko ibihugu bituranye na Congo birimo u Rwanda bifite umugambi wo gucamo ibice igihugu cye bik@@ akiy@@ om@@ ekaho .
Ni amagambo yamag@@ aniwe kure haba muri Leta ya Congo ndetse n' abandi bakurikiranira politiki y' akarere hafi .
Minisitiri w' Ububanyi n' Amahanga , Dr Vincent Biruta , aherutse kuvuga ko imvugo z' abanyapolitiki bamwe bo muri RDC ku Rwanda ziba@@ baje kuko ahanini n' ibyo bavuga ari ibintu biba bidafite insh@@ ingiro .
Ati " Ni ibintu bibabaje , wakw@@ iteguye ko ibyo bavuga biba bifite icyo bafite gifatika ariko nta gihari .
Ntabwo ari ubwa mbere bene ibi bibazo bibaho , hashize igihe hari abanyapolitiki bo muri RDC bumva ko kugira ngo abaturage babo bab@@ emere ari uko bavuga nabi u Rwanda .
Dr Biruta yavuze ko nta mugambi uhari wo kom@@ eka ibice bya Congo ku Rwanda kandi nta n' uz@@ igera ubaho .
U Rwanda na RDC bifitanye umubano mwiza cyane cyane nyuma y' aho F√©lix Tshisekedi atorewe kuyobora icyo gihugu , akavuga ko ar@@ ajwe ishinga no kubana neza n' ibihugu by' ibit@@ uranyi .
Minisitiri Mat@@ eke wa Uganda yahishuye ko at@@ emeranya n' amasezerano n' u Rwanda n' umugambi mushya bar@@ ufiteho
Mu gihe hashize iminsi mike hat@@ ekerezwa ko umubano w' u Rwanda na Uganda waba utangiye kugana mu cyerekezo kizima nyuma y' irekurwa ry' abanyarwanda icyenda bari bafung@@ iwe@@ yo binyuranyije n' amategeko , ibintu byabaye nk' ibis@@ ubira i Rud@@ ubi ubwo Umunyamabanga wa Leta Ushinzwe ubutwererane n' akarere , Phil@@ emon Mat@@ eke , yavugaga uburyo atemera amasezerano yasinywe hagati ya Uganda n' u Rwanda .
Mu gihe hashize iminsi mike hat@@ ekerezwa ko umubano w' u Rwanda na Uganda waba utangiye kugana mu cyerekezo kizima nyuma y' irekurwa ry' abanyarwanda icyenda bari bafung@@ iwe@@ yo binyuranyije n' amategeko , ibintu byabaye nk' ibis@@ ubira i Rud@@ ubi ubwo Umunyamabanga wa Leta Ushinzwe ubutwererane n' akarere , Phil@@ emon Mat@@ eke , yavugaga uburyo atemera amasezerano yasinywe hagati ya Uganda n' u Rwanda .
Ni amasezerano yasiny@@ iwe i Luanda muri Angola ku wa 21 Kanama 2019 , agamije gushakira umuti ibibazo u Rwanda rw@@ ashinj@@ aga icyo gihugu birimo gufunga abaturage barwo binyuranyije n' amategeko no kubakorera iyicarubozo , gushyigikira imitwe igamije kuruh@@ ungabany@@ iriza umutekano no kubangamira ubucuruzi bwarwo .
Mu butumwa yanditse kuri Twitter kuri uyu wa Kane , Mat@@ eke yahishuye ko kuva kera na kare atem@@ eraga amasezerano bas@@ inyanye n' u Rwanda agamije guhosha umwuka mubi uri hagati y' ibihugu byombi , mu gihe ari umwe mu bagombaga kuba bakurikirana uko ashyirwa mu bikorwa .
Yagize ati " Nab@@ uriye bagenzi banjye ko nta cyiza kiva mu gusinyana amasezerano n' ikibi .
Kug@@ arura amahoro ntib@@ yakunze kuri Ch@@ amb@@ er@@ la@@ in mu 19@@ 38 , ntabwo natwe biz@@ ashoboka .

Aha mu 19@@ 38 yashakaga kuvuga ku byabaye muri uwo mwaka hakor@@ waga inama z' inkur@@ ikir@@ ane hagati y' ibihugu by' u Bwongereza , u Bufaransa , n' u Butaliyani , bik@@ emerera u Budage bwari buyobowe na Adol@@ f Hitler kwiy@@ om@@ ekaho ibice bimwe bya C@@ z@@ ech@@ os@@ lov@@ ak@@ ia , mu buryo bwo kwirinda intambara .
Hitler yasabaga igice cya Sud@@ et@@ en@@ land , Nev@@ ille Ch@@ amb@@ er@@ la@@ in wari Minisitiri w' Intebe w' u Bwongereza afata iya mbere aza guhura n' uway@@ oboraga u Bufaransa , Edu@@ ard Dal@@ ad@@ ier na Ben@@ ito Mus@@ sol@@ ini wayoboraga u Butaliyani , bahurira i Munich na Hitler , bemeranya ko agace ka Sud@@ et@@ en@@ land kom@@ ekwa k' u Budage , bataha bahamya ko habonetse amahoro .
Nyuma y' amezi atanu Hitler yarenze ku byem@@ er@@ anyij@@ weho agaba igitero kuri C@@ z@@ ech@@ os@@ lov@@ ak@@ ia yose aray@@ ifata .
Nubwo Mat@@ eke atat@@ oboye ngo avuge izina ry' igihugu , ibyo Mat@@ eke yavuze bihura neza n' ibibazo birimo kuba hagati y' u Rwanda na Uganda .
Naho iby@@ ' abantu barashwe yavugaga bihuye n' uko kuri uyu wa Gatatu u Rwanda rw@@ ashyikirije Uganda umurambo w' umuturage wayo , Ndagijimana Theogene , warashwe n' inzego z' umutekano z' u Rwanda zam@@ ufatiye mu bikorwa bya magendu ashaka no kwinjiza ibiyobyabwenge mu gihugu , z@@ amuh@@ agarika akagerageza kuz@@ irwanya .
Amagambo ya Mat@@ eke an@@ ahura n' ay@@ ' umudepite Ruth Nan@@ kab@@ irwa , kuri uyu wa Gatatu wabwiye bagenzi be mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko ko Guverinoma ya Uganda ikwiye gukemura bwangu ikibazo ifitanye n' u Rwanda , ariko asa n' uca amarenga ku buryo bw@@ akoreshwa .

Mu biganiro biheruka guhuza intumwa z' u Rwanda na Uganda mu Ukuboza 2019 , u Rwanda rwagaragaje uburyo Mat@@ eke yari inyuma y' abarwanyi bagabye igitero i Musanze ahazwi nko mu Kinigi kig@@ ahitana abaturage 14 .
Ubwo bari ku ngingo zijyanye n' uko Uganda ifasha imitwe yitwaje intwaro , Nduhungirehe yatanze urugero rw' igitero cyabaye mu ijoro rishyira ku itariki ya Kane Ukwakira aho abarwanyi b' umutwe wa RUD Urunana bateye mu Kinigi .
Mu iperereza ryakozwe , hari ibikoresho byafashwe birimo na telefoni zigendanwa n' ubuhamya bwatanzwe n' abafashwe , byagaragaje uruhare rwa Uganda muri iki gitero .
Nduhungirehe ati " Ibyo byose bigaragaza ko uwari uyoboye icyo gitero ari uwitwa Phil@@ emon Mat@@ eke akaba Umunyamabanga wa leta ya Uganda ushinzwe ubutwererane bw' akarere .
B@@ yagaragajwe na za telefoni n' ubuhamya bwatanzwe n' abafashwe .
" Hari n' uwitwa Nsh@@ imiye wiyita Govern@@ or ushinzwe ibikorwa byihariye muri RUD Urunana , atuye hariya mu Karere ka Kis@@ oro n' umuryango we , byagaragaye ko akunda kujya muri Kivu y' Amajyaruguru ahitwa B@@ enza gutegura ibitero kandi ko ariwe wakor@@ anaga bya hafi na Phil@@ emon Mat@@ eke .
Urwo ni urugero rumwe nat@@ anze ariko hari n' izindi nyinshi twatanze zigaragaza ko bag@@ ikomeza guha urubuga abat@@ urwanya .
Si ubwa mbere Mat@@ eke avuzwe mu bikorwa bigamije guhungabanya umutekano w' u Rwanda , kuko byavuzwe ko mu Ukuboza 2018 yakor@@ anyaga inama yahuje FDLR na RNC i Kampala , ngo bateg@@ ure igikorwa gih@@ uriweho cya gisirikare ku Rwanda nk' uko La For@@ ge Bazeye na Theophile Abega bari bahagarariye FDLR muri iyo nama bab@@ ivuze nyuma yo gufatirwa ku mupaka wa Bun@@ agana basubiye mu birindiro muri RDC .
Dus@@ ubize amaso inyuma
Ubush@@ otoranyi bwa Uganda ku Rwanda si ubwa vuba , ndetse mu myaka yashize h@@ avuyemo uguk@@ oz@@ anyaho kw@@ abereye muri Repubulika ya Demokarasi ya Congo , by@@ avuyemo intambara ya Kisangani yarangiye RPA itsinze ingabo za Uganda , ibintu byababaje Uganda ku rwego rukomeye .
G@@ utsind@@ irwa i Kisangani byatumye abaturage ba Uganda n' Inteko Ishinga Amategeko bashyira igitutu ku bushobozi bwa Museveni no ku hazaza he .
Muri kwa gusuzugura u Rwanda , abadepite barak@@ ariye Museveni ariko baguma no kw@@ ikoma Guverinoma y' u Rwanda , nk' uko raporo ya International C@@ ris@@ is Group yo mu 2000 ibigaragaza .
Icyo gihe Museveni yabonye ko uburyo bwo guc@@ ubya abaturage be ari ukw@@ ibasira RPA mu magambo at@@ yaye .
Mu ijambo ryo ku wa 30 Kanama 1999 , Museveni yabaye nk' uw@@ ikura mu bibazo aby@@ egeka ku bandi .
Ati " Icyo n@@ abasobanurira ni uko abavandimwe bacu muri RPA batabashije gukura ngo bamenye uko ibintu bimwe na bimwe bikorwa .
B@@ umva ko kunyura iya bugufi hano na hariya biz@@ abageza ku ntego yabo .
Ikindi maze iminsi numva ni uko RPA yashatse kwigarurira Congo ariko ko turimo kubak@@ oma imbere .
" Ku ruhande rwacu dush@@ ishikajwe no kongerera ubushobozi abanye - Congo ariko bigaragara ko Abanyarwanda bataby@@ ishimiye .
Ariko nubwo twaba tub@@ angamiye imigambi bafite muri Congo , ni gute bumva ko batug@@ abaho ibitero ngo bir@@ angirire aho ?
Ni ukureba hafi cyane .
Igisirikare cya Uganda nticy@@ igeze cyakira inshuro cy@@ akubiswe n' Abanyarwanda , aho bumvaga ko ishema n' icyubahiro byabo byah@@ ungabany@@ ijwe , ibitangazamakuru by@@ anz@@ ika ko UPDF yatsinzwe ndetse abasirikare bayo barenga 200 bagapfa .
Raporo ya IC@@ G ivuga ko hahise hatangira inama z' ibanga i Kampala zik@@ itabirwa n' abasirikare bakiri mu mirimo n' abas@@ ezerewe , ngo " bashak@@ ishe uburyo bwo kwihimura ku cyo bafataga nk' ubugambanyi bw' abari bafatanyije n' u Rwanda .
Hari aho yagize iti " Abasirikare bakuru mu Ngabo za Uganda bavuga ko umubano n' u Rwanda ut@@ azongera na rimwe kuba nk' uko wahoze nyuma y' ib@@ yabereye i Kisangani .

Ubwa mbere hari ubwo has@@ iny@@ waga amasezerano ya Luanda , ubwa kabiri by@@ ashing@@ irwa ku magambo ya Museveni asoza umwaka wa 2019 .
Mu butumwa yashyize ku rukuta rwe rwa Twitter mbere y' uko tw@@ injira mu mwaka mushya wa 2020 , Museveni yavuze ko yakiriye intumwa ye Ambasaderi Ad@@ onia A@@ ye@@ bare uherutse mu Rwanda afite ubutumwa bugenewe Perezida Kagame ku mubano w' ibihugu byombi .

Ubutumwa bwa Museveni ku kibazo cya Uganda n' u Rwanda biragoye ko umuntu yabw@@ izera 100 % , ngo y@@ ishyir@@ emo ko hari ikig@@ iye gukorwa kuko mu gihe yab@@ wandik@@ aga , ibimenyetso bigaragaza ibih@@ abanye n' ibyo yavugaga .

Ni nako Uganda kandi yakomeje umubano wayo n' imitwe igamije guhungabanya umutekano w' u Rwanda irimo RNC na FDLR ndetse ir@@ in@@ angira ubwo yasabaga kubahiriza amasezerano Museveni yasinywe .
Ibi nibyo byatumye intumwa z' u Rwanda na Uganda zin@@ anirwa kumvikana mu biganiro biheruka kubera i Kampala .

Ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Min@@ nes@@ ota buk@@ urikiranye umuhanzi R Kelly ku byaha byo gukoresha ibikorwa by' uburaya umukobwa utarageza imyaka y' ubuk@@ ure .
Ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Min@@ nes@@ ota buk@@ urikiranye umuhanzi R Kelly ku byaha byo gukoresha ibikorwa by' uburaya umukobwa utarageza imyaka y' ubuk@@ ure .
Umuvugizi w' ubushinjacyaha mu Karere ka H@@ enn@@ ep@@ in , Mike Fre@@ eman niwe watangaje ibyaha bish@@ injwa Robert Sylv@@ ester Kelly w' imyaka 50 .
Fre@@ eman yavuze ko ibyo R .
Kelly ashinjwa byabaye muri Nyakanga 2001 nyuma y' aho umwana w' umukobwa wari ufite imyaka 17 yamusabye ko yamus@@ igira is@@ inya y' urwibutso [ aut@@ ogr@@ ap@@ h ] .
Kelly ngo yasinyiye uyu mwana an@@ amuha nomero ze za telefone .
Ubwo yamuh@@ amagaraga yamusabye kum@@ usanga kuri hoteli yari arimo , yakirwa n' umugabo yak@@ etse ko bari uwo mu itsinda rye .
Iki kirego kivuga ko R .
Kelly ubwo yahuraga n' uyu mwana baganiriye umwanya muto , ubundi amw@@ ishyura $ 200 kugira ngo amub@@ yin@@ ire .
B@@ emeranyije kuri ayo mafaranga , maze am@@ ukuramo imyenda nyuma nawe akuramo iye , agenda amuk@@ or@@ akora uko yam@@ ubyin@@ iraga .
Umubano wabo war@@ akomeje R .
Kelly amuha itike yo kujya mu ny@@ anya y' icyubahiro mu gitaramo cyari kigenewe abar@@ engeje imyaka 18 , yinj@@ ir@@ ayo at@@ ishyuye cyangwa ngo yerek@@ ane n' indangamuntu ye .
Uyu mukobwa yag@@ annye inzego z' ubutabera muri Mutarama uyu mwaka , ubwo ibindi birego byari bikomeje kwis@@ uka kuri R .
Umuvugizi w' ubushinjacyaha , Mike Fre@@ eman yavuze ko bibabaje kuba R Kelly yarakoresheje ubw@@ amamare bwe mu kwangiza abana b' abakobwa .
Ntabwo har@@ amenyekana igihe R Kelly azag@@ erezwa imbere y' urukiko rwo muri Leta ya Min@@ nes@@ ota kuko hari izindi nkiko nazo z@@ imuk@@ urikirana .
Umwe mu bunganira R Kelly yahakanye ibyaha ashinjwa avuga ko ari abashaka gukomeza kur@@ unda ibyaha ku muk@@ iriya wabo .
Yash@@ idik@@ anyije niba koko baran@@ ahuye nubwo mu bivugwa ngo atumva icyaha cy' ubusambanyi kirimo .
Ikirego cyo muri Leta ya Min@@ nes@@ ota kije nyuma y' ibindi byinshi uyu muhanzi yagiye ashinjwa muri Leta zitandukanye , aho akurikiranyweho ibyaha bijyanye no gusambanya abana batar@@ uzuza imyaka y' ubuk@@ ure .
Ubushinjacyaha bwa Leta za Il@@ lin@@ ois na New York bw@@ amush@@ injije gushaka abagore ajyana mu buraya , kwishyura abantu kugira ngo bamuh@@ ish@@ ire no gutanga amafaranga kugira ngo asub@@ izwe amashusho yamug@@ aragazaga asambana n' abana batarageza ku myaka y' ubuk@@ ure .
Muri Gashyantare yahakanye ibyaha 10 yashinjwaga n' ubushinjacyaha bwo muri Leta ya Il@@ lin@@ ois ar@@ afungwa aza kurekurwa atanze ingwate ya ibihumbi $ 100 .

Abagore n' abakobwa bihariye 95 % by' Abanyarwanda bahuye n' icuruzwa ry' abantu
Ubushakashatsi bushya bwagaragaje ko icuruzwa ry' abantu ari ikibazo gihangayikishije u Rwanda n' Isi muri rusange , ndetse ko bukorerwa umubare munini w' urubyiruko rwig@@ anjemo abakobwa kurusha abahungu .
Ubushakashatsi bushya bwagaragaje ko icuruzwa ry' abantu ari ikibazo gihangayikishije u Rwanda n' Isi muri rusange , ndetse ko bukorerwa umubare munini w' urubyiruko rwig@@ anjemo abakobwa kurusha abahungu .
Ubushakashatsi ku kibazo cy' icuruzwa ry' abantu mu Rwanda bw@@ amuritswe kuri uyu wa 19 Nyakanga 2019 , bwakozwe n' Umuryango Never Ag@@ ain Rwanda hagati ya 2017 na 2018 .
Imibare yatanzwe n' Urwego rw' abinjira n' abas@@ ohoka yagaragaje ko mu Rwanda ahanini abacur@@ uzwa bah@@ anyuzwa bajyanwe mu bindi bihugu , kuko abah@@ akurwa ari bo bake .
Mu bantu 5@@ 15 bacur@@ ujwe higanjemo Abarundi , bagera kuri 3@@ 23 bingana na 62 .
Harimo kandi Ab@@ anye - Congo 77 ( 15 % ) , Abanyarwanda 70 ( 13 .
6 % ) n' abantu 45 ( 8 .
7 ) bo mu bindi bihugu .
Ur@@ ebeye ku gitsina , abagore n' abakobwa bari 400 ( 77 .
67 % ) naho ab@@ ' igitsina gabo ari 11@@ 5 ( 22 .
Ku ruh@@ anda rw' u Rwanda , ubu bushakashatsi bwerekana ko mu bacur@@ ujwe , 95 .
24 % ari ab@@ ' igitsina gore , 87 .

Abakoze ubushakashatsi bas@@ obanuye ko abajya gucuruzwa akenshi bab@@ eshywa ko bagiye guhabwa akazi keza , kwiga n' ibindi , bag@@ ez@@ wayo ntiba@@ bib@@ one cyangwa bagash@@ orwa mu bikorwa by' urukozasoni n' ibindi bigira ingaruka ku buzima bwabo .
Zimwe mu mpamvu zituma ubucuruzi bw' abantu bwiyongera harimo imibereho mibi , ubukene , ubushomeri mu rubyiruko , igitutu cy' umuryango , abab@@ eshywa ko bagiye kurih@@ irwa amashuri n' ibindi .
Umuyobozi wa Never Ag@@ ain , Dr Nkurunziza R@@ yar@@ asa Joseph , yavuze ko hakenewe ubuvugizi kugira ngo abanyarwanda bamenye uko icuruzwa ry' abantu rikorwa , ingaruka rigira n' uko bar@@ yirinda .
Ati " Icyo dusaba ni ukugira ngo habeho ihan@@ ahana ry' amakuru cyane cyane mu kigo gishinzwe abinjira n' abas@@ ohoka , Urwego rw' Ubugenzacyaha , Polisi n' urw@@ ' Ubutabera , kuko kugira ngo iki kibazo gikem@@ uke ni uko abantu baba bafite amakuru yuzuye .
Yasabye ko hakwiye no kujyaho ikigo gifasha mu is@@ anamitima ku bantu bah@@ ungabany@@ irijwe mu icuruzwa ry' abantu , abat@@ eshejwe ishuri bagafashwa kur@@ isubiramo .
Umuyobozi w' Ishami rishinzwe ubutabera mpuzamahanga muri Minisiteri y' Ubutabera , Umur@@ ungi Provid@@ ence , yavuze ko icuruzwa ry' abantu atari ikibazo cy' u Rwanda gusa ahubwo cyugarije Isi yose .
Ati " Ib@@ ivuye muri ubu bushakashatsi bizadufasha gushyira muri gahunda no guteg@@ anye icyakorwa mu rwego rwo kurwanya icuruzwa ry' abantu .
Umur@@ ungi yavuze ko imiryango ariyo ifite uruhare rukomeye kuko bigaragara ko abajya gucuruzwa bajyanwa n' abo bafitanye isano .
Ishyirahamwe mpuzamahanga ryita ku murimo ( IL@@ O ) riheruka kugaragaza ko abantu barenga miliyoni 24 .
9 barimo abagabo , abagore n' abana bash@@ owe mu bucuruzi bw' abantu mu 2017 .
Umuz@@ imu was@@ aritse abarwanya u Rwanda uz@@ orohera Twagiramungu na Rusesabagina bihuje ?
Umuny@@ apolitiki utavuga rumwe na Leta y' u Rwanda , Faustin Twagiramungu , yih@@ uje ku mugaragaro n' Ihuriro MRCD , riyobowe na Paul Rusesabagina , mu bufatanye bwiswe ubwo guhuza imbaraga mu kurwanya ubutegetsi bw' u Rwanda , hakoreshejwe inzira zose .

Amasezerano hagati y' ishyaka RD@@ I Rwanda Rw@@ iza , rya Twagiramungu na MRCD , igizwe na RR@@ M ya Nsabimana Callixte ' Sankara ' , ufung@@ iwe mu Rwanda , P@@ DR Ih@@ umure na CNRD Ubw@@ iyunge ya Gen .

Ifite ishami rya gisirikare ryitwa FLN , ikaba ari umutwe w' iterabwoba wag@@ abye ibitero mu Majyepfo y' u Rwanda , big@@ ahitana abaturage icyenda , 19 bag@@ akomereka ndetse n' imitungo myinshi igas@@ ah@@ urwa indi ik@@ angizwa .
Uwari umuvugizi w' uyu mutwe Nsabimana yumvikanye ku maradiyo ya BBC na VOA , n' imbuga nka YouTube yig@@ amba ibyo bitero , avuga ko ari ibya FLN iyobowe na Habimana Hamad@@ a .
Umus@@ esenguzi mu bya politiki y' ibiyaga bigari , akaba impuguke mu itangazamakuru , Albert Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa , avuga ko kuba Twagiramungu yahisemo kwihuza ku mugaragaro n' umutwe w' iterabwoba , MRCD , bisobanura ko atakiri muri politiki gusa ahubwo yinjiye no mu iterabwoba .
Avuga ko Twagiramungu yifuza guhirika ubuyobozi bw' u Rwanda ariko akaba yarabuze uko abigenza , bityo akaba yih@@ uje n' abandi babim@@ azemo iminsi , ariko ku bwe iri huriro ntacyo ryag@@ eraho .
Ati " Ni amagambo gusa , ni uk@@ uvugira kuri radiyo hirya no hino ariko ntacyo bivuze , nta n' ikintu gifatika gihari " " " " .
In@@ enge kuri Rusesabagina na Twagiramungu
Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa avuga ko aba bagabo bose bafite inenge iz@@ ingiye ku ' bushobozi buke ' butuma ubufatanye bwabo ntacyo bwag@@ eraho .
Mbere ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 , Paul Rusesabagina yari umuntu usanzwe , yavukiye i Mur@@ ama ya Gitarama ku wa 15 Kamena 195@@ 4 , ariko nyuma yagiye gutura i Bruxelles mu Bubiligi na Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Uburyo abantu bamuzi bw@@ ahinduwe cyane na filimi Hotel Rwanda yamuk@@ in@@ weho nk' uwar@@ okoye abantu 12@@ 68 muri H@@ √¥@@ tel des Mille Collines , abay@@ ob@@ ejwe nayo batangira kumuh@@ und@@ agaz@@ aho ibihembo kugeza kuri ' Presid@@ ent@@ ial Med@@ al Award of Fre@@ ed@@ om ' , yahawe na Perezida George W .
Bush wa Amerika mu Ugushyingo 2005 .
Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa agaruka ku mateka ya Rusesabagina akavuga ko atari umunyapolitiki , ahubwo yari umuntu wakoreraga h@@ √¥@@ tel akaza kugirwa igitangaza na filimi bityo agatangira kwibaza ko uwo muntu uri muri filime ari we kandi atari we .
Ati " Ni ukw@@ is@@ umbuk@@ uruza gusa kandi nta bushobozi afite uretse ko yabonye abantu bamw@@ umva kuko bibaza ko ari wawundi wo muri filime ariko mu banyarwanda nta kintu avuze , ntacyo bamuz@@ iho uretse ibyo ah@@ wih@@ w@@ isa mu maradiyo gusa n' ahandi " " " " .
Ak@@ om@@ ereza kuri Twagiramungu , akavuga ko we yabaye umunyapolitiki kuva kera ariko ubu akaba ari ' umunyapolitiki was@@ igajwe inyuma n' amateka ' , kuko uko u Rwanda rwateye imbere ntacyo bim@@ ubwiye akiri mu bya kera yari yar@@ amenyereye ku ngoma zindi .
Mu nteruro imwe Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa ati " Nta hantu bishobora kubageza kuko nta ruhare bafite no ku banyarwanda " " " " .
Umuz@@ imu was@@ aritse abarwanya u Rwanda baz@@ aw@@ ukira ?
Si ubwa mbere abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi bw' u Rwanda , bifatanyije bagashyiraho amahuriro ngo bah@@ uze imbaraga bagere ku mugambi wabo ariko bikarangira bish@@ wany@@ utse ntacyo big@@ ezeho .
Ingero ni nyinshi cyane .
Ntawe utazi uko RNC ya Kayumba Nyamwasa yash@@ wany@@ utse .
U@@ guterana amagambo hagati ya Dr Th√©og√®ne Rudasingwa na Kayumba Nyamwasa , bari bahuriye muri RNC , mbere y' uko bac@@ ikamo ibice , byatumye n' abo biz@@ ezaga ibitangaza bacika intege .
Aha niho hav@@ utsemo amashyaka at@@ emewe mu Rwanda arimo na RR@@ M ya Nsabimana , nayo yac@@ itsemo ibice mbere y' ifatwa rye kubera ubwumvikane buke , gus@@ uzug@@ urana no kutemera uburyo abayobozi bishyira mu myanya .
Hari kandi n' amatiku hagati y' abasivili n' abahoze mu gisirikare .
RR@@ M igizwe n' abantu ahanini bavuye mu Rwanda bahunze ibyaha bakoze cyangwa andi makosa .
Twagiramungu ubwe nawe yashinze ihuriro ry' amashyaka atavuga rumwe na Leta y' u Rwanda ( C@@ PC ) , ryari rigizwe na FDLR , UD@@ R , RD@@ I , CN@@ R , na PS Imberakuri , igice cya gatatu .
Abar@@ igize baje kun@@ anir@@ anwa nawe bamushinja igitugu .
Muri rusange iyo ugiye kwitegereza umuz@@ imu was@@ aritse aya mashyaka , ni ug@@ up@@ ingana no kur@@ yana , buri wese arw@@ anira kuba ku isonga no guhabwa iby@@ ubahiro by' umukuru w' ishyaka cyangwa uz@@ ayobora igihugu igihe bageze ku butegetsi .
Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa yongeraho izindi mpamvu abash@@ inga aya mah@@ uriro ntacyo bageraho ari uko ik@@ ibag@@ enza ari inyungu zabo bwite , kwitwaza iturufu y' amoko n' intege nke basanganywe .
Ati " Ubundi mu mvugo zabo usanga nka Rusesabagina afite akantu ko kuzana iby@@ ' amoko , RNC usanga ikibazo bafite ari umuyobozi mukuru .
Ni ug@@ uhuza gusa ariko ubona ko bafite intege ziri hasi cyane , bakibaza ko guhuza imbaraga byatuma bazamura urwego rw' imbaraga zabo ariko akenshi ubona ko kuba ari abantu bifitiye gahunda zabo bwite , birangira akenshi bash@@ wanye kuko hari aho bataz@@ ahuza " " " " .
Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa akomeza agira ati " Ntiba@@ fite ingengabitekerezo ifatika yatuma babona n' imfashanyo , bir@@ angirira aho .
Mu by' ukuri ( Twagiramungu ) , aba ashaka kwihuza n' abandi kuko nta bushobozi na buke afite , niwe wenyine wibaza ko izina gusa rik@@ urura ariko hashize imyaka 25 uriya muntu ntabwo azwi , ntawe yak@@ urura , nta na ben@@ ewabo yak@@ urura .
Avuga ko FPR Inkotanyi yash@@ obotse bitewe no guhuza mu bitekerezo byari bifitiye akamaro abanyarwanda bose yaba abari impunzi n' abandi bari mu gihugu babaho mu buzima bw' ingoma ya Habyarimana .
Ati " Niyo mpamvu FPR yak@@ uruye abantu n' ubushobozi bw' abo bantu .
Ikindi harimo n' abantu bafite ubunararibonye bw' uko niba byanze muri politiki hari uko babikora bakurikije ubushobozi bwo gushoza intambara .
Abandi ntabyo bafite , akenshi ban@@ afashwa n' abantu bashaka kugirira u Rwanda nabi ariko nabo kubera aho u Rwanda rugeze nta ngaruka yindi bifite uretse guk@@ erereza iterambere ryabo " " " " .
U Budage ntib@@ wakw@@ icarana n' abahoze ari aba - N@@ azi
Twagiramungu n' abandi bafatanyije kurwanya ubutegetsi bw' u Rwanda , ntibas@@ iba kumvikana bavuga ko baz@@ agaruka mu Rwanda habaye ibiganiro .
Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa asanga ntaho ibi biganiro byah@@ era kuko u Rwanda rud@@ aheza kandi ruh@@ ora rush@@ ishikariza impunzi n' abari mu mahanga gutaha , bityo n' abo bashaka ibiganiro bakwiye gutaha niba hari icyo bahindura ku cyerekezo cy' u Rwanda , bakag@@ ikora .
Icyakora avuga ko harimo n' abantu kuganira na bo byag@@ ereranywa no kuvuga uti ' u Budage bw' iki gihe bukwiye kwicarana n' abahoze ari aba - N@@ azi cya gihe cya Hitler ' kuko abuzukuru babo babis@@ abye .
Abo Twagiramungu yifatanyije nabo harimo abashyir@@ iweho impapuro mpuzamahanga zibat@@ a muri yombi , Rud@@ ats@@ imburwa avuga ko nta kabuza uyu musaza agomba gufatwa nk' umut@@ er@@ abwoba kuko kuba yifatanyije nabo bivuze ko yemera ibyo bakora .
Kugeza ubu ikibaz@@ wa ni ik@@ idasanzwe ubufatanye bwa MRCD na RD@@ I Rwanda Rw@@ iza buz@@ anye ku buryo bidatinze abantu bataz@@ umva iri huriro ryatewe n' umuz@@ imu was@@ aritse abarwanya u Rwanda , nabo bag@@ acik@@ amo ibice .
Big@@ enda bite iyo umudepite ageze mu Nteko nt@@ atange ibitekerezo ?
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cy@@ umvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yar@@ itor@@ eye ngo amuh@@ agarar@@ ire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo by' impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu ba@@ bita intumwa za rubanda .
Iyo havuzwe Umudepite nta kindi cy@@ umvikana mu matwi ya benshi , uretse uwo umuturage aba yar@@ itor@@ eye ngo amuh@@ agarar@@ ire mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko atanga ibitekerezo by' impinduka zikenewe , ni nayo mpamvu ba@@ bita intumwa za rubanda .
Mu nshingano z' intumwa za rubanda harimo gutora amategeko abar@@ eye abaturage , kugenzura ibikorwa bya guverinoma , kwemeza abayobozi runaka , hari n' ibihugu baba bafite inshingano zo gutora abakuru b' igihugu .
Nubwo baba barat@@ owe n' abaturage ngo babah@@ agarar@@ ire , mu bihugu bimwe birimo n' u Rwanda , usanga hari abaturage bavuga ko baheruka babat@@ ora ntibaz@@ ongere ku@@ baca ir@@ yera cyangwa bagat@@ ora amategeko at@@ aban@@ ogeye .
Tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 ubwo yakiraga indahiro z' Abadepite , Perezida Paul Kagame , yavuze ko bagomba kujya begera abaturage , bakabikora nk' uko babigenza iyo babash@@ ak@@ amo amajwi .
Ati " Igihe mwese mw@@ amaze mw@@ iyamamaza hirya no hino mu gihugu , mw@@ abon@@ anye n' Abanyarwanda , uko mw@@ abag@@ ezeho m@@ ubash@@ ak@@ aho amajwi ariko bizakomeza kubag@@ eraho mu@@ basanga , m@@ ufatanya gukemura ibibazo bafite .
Mu nteko habamo imirimo myinshi irimo kwiga imishinga y' amategeko , kuy@@ isuzuma , kuy@@ itangaho ibitekerezo n' ibindi .
Akenshi abaturage bamenya ubushobozi bw' umudepite batoye bitewe n' uburyo abavug@@ anira , ibitekerezo atanga ku ngingo zitandukanye ziz@@ anwa mu Nteko , kubasura n' ibindi .
Hari ibihugu umudepite ugeze mu nteko ntiy@@ ongere kumvikana ku ngingo zib@@ angamiye abaturage agaragazwa , byaba na ngombwa akaba yah@@ agarikwa .
Nko mu 2018 muri Kenya , ikinyamakuru The Stand@@ ard cyas@@ ohoye urutonde rw' abadepite batajya bavuga mu Nteko .
H@@ avugwaga ko hari Abadepite bicara mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ntiba@@ be batekereza umushinga w@@ afasha abaturage ahubwo icyo bakora , bikaba gusa gushyigikira imishinga yavuzwe n' abandi .
Iki kibazo cy@@ azamuwe na bamwe mu badepite muri iki gihugu , batangiye bij@@ uj@@ uta bavuga ko hari bagenzi babo bah@@ it@@ agamo kwis@@ ohokera , mu gihe abandi babaga bageze ku ngingo zikomeye zo gut@@ orerwamo amategeko .
Depite Justin B@@ ed@@ an Nj@@ oka Mut@@ uri yabwiye abanyamakuru ati " Ntabwo n@@ ishimye kuko hari abadepite bagenzi bacu usanga birirwa bavuga ko bishimira ibyo bagezeho mu nteko , mu gihe mu by' ukuri ntacyo bigeze bakora .
Yavuze ko hari bamwe usanga bat@@ agaragara mu gihe barimo gushaka gushyiraho itegeko runaka , nyamara nyuma ry@@ ajya gutorwa ugasanga batangiye kwij@@ uj@@ uta kandi batar@@ igeze bagaragara mbere ngo bar@@ itang@@ eho ibitekerezo .
Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Kenya yavuze ko 70 % by' abayigize wasangaga nta jambo bafata ngo batange ibitekerezo , bamwe muri bakaba bar@@ avugaga ko babiterwa n' uko babaga bakiri bashya mu nshingano .
Mu Rwanda bihagaze gute ?
Kugeza ubu Inteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda igizwe n' Imitwe ibiri , Umutwe w' Abadepite na Sena .
Kuva tariki 19 Nzeri 2018 umutwe w' abadepite wabonye abadepite bashya 80 bari muri manda iz@@ ageza mu 20@@ 23 , naho kuva mu Ukwakira 2019 hatowe abasenateri , kugeza ubu bose hamwe ni 26 .
Nubwo bitoroshye kumenya imikorere ya buri mudepite , iyo uganiriye na bamwe muri aba bakubwira ko nubwo hari bamwe batavuga , ngo ni uburenganzira bwabo cyane ko nta tegeko rihari ri@@ bategeka kuvuga .
Depite , Dr Frank Habineza , usanzwe ari n' Umuyobozi w' Ishyaka R@@ iharanira Demokarasi no kurengera ibidukikije ( DG@@ PR ) , yabwiye IGIHE ati " Abadepite bose bafite uburenganzira bungana imbere y' amategeko , nta mudepite kandi ub@@ uzwa kugira igitekerezo atanga , buri wese afite uburenganzira bw' iminota ingana , burya umuntu kutavuga ni umutimanama we .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ubwabo nk' abadepite badashobora kwicara ngo ban@@ enge umudepite runaka utajya utanga ibitekerezo , keretse wenda bikor@@ ewe mu mutwe wa politike at@@ urukamo .
Ati " Ibyo byakorwa n' amashyaka kuko buri shyaka rigira umuh@@ wit@@ uzi .
Nk@@ ' ubu twe nubwo turi babiri mu nteko ariko dufite umuh@@ wit@@ uzi ari we njye , ubu mfite uburenganzira bwo gukurikirana umudepite wo mu ishyaka ryanjye iyo nta gitekerezo atanga cyangwa ntacyo avuga , nd@@ amubaza nti ese wowe ko mbona utavuga wabaye iki ?
n' ahandi ubwo ni uko babikora .
Dr Habineza avuga ko ku giti cye intego yajyanye mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko , ni uko buri gihe aba yiteguye kugira icyo yavuga gifasha umuturage .
Ati " Nta tegeko ry@@ ac@@ aho ntar@@ ivuzeho kandi na mugenzi wanjye uba muri PAC agomba kureba uko amafaranga akoreshwa neza .
Kuva mu 2008 , Depite Nyirah@@ irwa V@@ ener@@ anda ari mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda .
Yabwiye IGIHE ko abantu bashobora kwibeshya ko hari abadepite batavuga kandi iyo bari muri komisiyo batanga ibitekerezo .
Ati " Burya hari ibintu abantu batazi , mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko akazi g@@ akorwa mu byiciro bitandukanye , hari imirimo ikorerwa muri komisiyo abadepite bakajya impaka ku mategeko , nyuma akaz@@ ashyikirizwa inteko rusange , aha ni naho abaturage bose baba babyumva kuri radiyo .
" Hari abantu benshi usanga bazi ko dutangira akazi saa cyenda mu gihe harimo inteko rusange ariko siko biri .
T@@ uba tw@@ atangiriye muri komisiyo saa tatu ik@@ ageza saa sita , nyuma saa cyenda tukajya mu nteko rusange .
Nyirah@@ irwa yavuze ko muri ayo matsinda , hari abantu usanga batanga ibitekerezo , ntiba@@ bit@@ ange mu nteko rusange .
Ati " Hari abadepite usanga bavuga cyane mu mirimo ya komisiyo , mu nteko rusange burya hag@@ eramo iby@@ as@@ uzum@@ iwe muri za komisiyo ugasanga mu nteko rusange nt@@ avuze , ariko hari n' abandi bavuga hose .
Icyakora , yemeza ko hashobora kuba n' ut@@ atanga ibitekerezo aho h@@ ombi kuko iyo bageze mu nteko , nta muntu babwira ngo azag@@ ende avuge cyane .
Ati " Nta muntu uza kuguha amabwiriza ngo vuga , wan@@ amara rwose imyaka itanu ut@@ avuze kandi nta waz@@ abik@@ ubaza .
Depite , Sheikh Harerimana Musa Fazil , Visi Perezida ushinzwe Imari n' Abakozi mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda umutwe w' abadepite , yabwiye IGIHE ko kugeza ubu nta tegeko rihana umudepite ut@@ atanze ibitekerezo , bityo ko ut@@ abikoze nta tegeko aba yishe .
Agira ati " Nta cyaha gihari iyo ut@@ avuze kuko inteko ikorera mu mategeko , iyaba hari itegeko rivuga ngo niba ut@@ avuze umwaka wose bigenda gutya , icyo gihe twar@@ yubahiriza ariko noneho ubwo nta tegeko rihari , ubwo nabyo bir@@ emewe , ik@@ itab@@ ujijwe n' amategeko kiba cy@@ emewe .
Yavuze ko gahunda nyinshi mu nteko zibera muri za komisiyo , ku buryo hari abadepite benshi baba bar@@ atanze ibitekerezo , byagera mu nteko rusange akumva nta mpamvu yo kongera kuvuga .
Sheikh Harerimana yavuze ko bari kwiga ku buryo n' ibiganiro byab@@ eye muri za Komisiyo byajya bica kuri radiyo kugira ngo abaturage babashe gukurikirana ibikorwa by' Inteko n' imikorere y' abadepite batoye .
Ati " T@@ wamaze kuganira n' ubuyobozi bwa RBA ngo turebe ukuntu n' impaka z@@ abereye muri Komisiyo , rimwe na rimwe z@@ ajya ziny@@ ura kuri radiyo Rwanda Inteko , ibyo turimo kubig@@ anira biz@@ adut@@ wara amafaranga kandi ntar@@ aboneka ariko niwo murongo dushaka kuz@@ akoreramo .
Muri Uganda mu 2016 hasohotse urutonde rw' abadepite batajya bagaragara mu batanga ibitekerezo ku ngingo zireba abaturage , nyamara ari bo bahagarariye .
Mu badepite 4@@ 27 bagize Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Uganda , 82 ngo nta jambo na rimwe bari bak@@ avuze , 51 bari baravuze ijambo rimwe .
Mu 2011 , mu Bwongereza ibinyamakuru byas@@ ohoye urutonde rw' abadepite b' aban@@ ebwe .
Icyo gihe bash@@ ingiraga ku mubare w' inama abadepite bakoranaga n' abaturage bo mu duce bahagarariye .

Bar@@ inga ku cyiswe " bal@@ kan@@ isation " y' u Rwanda kuri RDC
Ijambo " bal@@ kan@@ isation " rimaze kuba intero n' iny@@ ikirizo mu mvugo y' abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida F√©lix Tshisekedi yat@@ orerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Ijambo " bal@@ kan@@ isation " rimaze kuba intero n' iny@@ ikirizo mu mvugo y' abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo , kuva Perezida F√©lix Tshisekedi yat@@ orerwa kuyobora iki gihugu .
Aba batifuza ko amahoro agaruka muri RDC , bakomeje guhimba ikinyoma ko u Rwanda rushaka kwig@@ arura Uburasirazuba bwayo , bagamije kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda n' Ab@@ anye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda .
Ib@@ ivugwa bisa no kureba filimi mbarankuru y' intambara zabaye mu kinyejana cya 20 mu Burayi bw' Amajyepfo , mu gace kiswe ' les Bal@@ kan@@ s ' , ubu kigizwe n' ibihugu nka Bul@@ gar@@ ie , Cro@@ ati@@ e , u Bug@@ iriki , Ro@@ uman@@ ie , Slov@@ √©n@@ ie , Al@@ ban@@ ie , Bos@@ n@@ ie - Her@@ z@@ √©g@@ ov@@ ine , K@@ os@@ ov@@ o , Mac@@ √©d@@ o@@ ine y' Amajyaruguru , Mont@@ √©n√©g@@ ro , Serb@@ ie na Tur@@ qu@@ ie ; byari byar@@ igar@@ uriwe n' Ubwami bw' Abami bwa Ot@@ tom@@ an , buk@@ abir@@ emamo uduh@@ ugu twinshi .
Igit@@ andukanye muri uyu mwaka wa 2020 , ni uko ibi bivug@@ irwa mu mihanda ya Kinshasa , aho aba@@ biy@@ oboye bad@@ akomoka muri Hong@@ rie cyangwa Turikiya , bahora baririmba bati " bal@@ kan@@ isation ntik@@ abe kuri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Mu Karere k' Ibiyaga Big@@ ari , ijambo ' bal@@ kan@@ isation ' ryatangiye kuh@@ umvikana mu mpera y' imyaka ya 1990 , ubwo u Rwanda na Uganda byat@@ eraga icyahoze cyitwa Za@@ √Ø@@ re .
Abaz@@ ay@@ irwa bari bafite ubwoba ko abaturanyi babo babiri bagiye kwisubiza ibice bah@@ oranye mbere y' uko Abany@@ aburayi big@@ abag@@ abanya Afurika , ariko ntiby@@ igeze biba .
Iyi mitekerereze yongeye kumvikana nyuma y' aho Joseph Kabila agiriye ku butegetsi mu 2001 .
Abam@@ urwanya bavugaga ko afite inkomoko mu Rwanda kandi akaba afite uruhare mu mugambi mpuzamahanga wo gucamo ibice RDC , ibice byayo by' Uburasirazuba bikize ku mabuye y' agaciro bikom@@ ekwa ku Rwanda .
Kujya ku butegetsi kwa F√©lix Tshisekedi bigaragara ko ntacyo byahinduye .
Ubu iyo nt@@ ero n' iny@@ ikirizo biri kuzamurwa n' Ihuriro ry' Amashyaka atavuga rumwe n' Ubutegetsi ya L@@ amuka ririmo na Martin Fayulu w@@ atsinzwe mu matora y' umukuru w' igihugu aheruka .
