Yaba L@@ amuka na Kiliziya ntibigeze bemera ko Fayulu yatsinzwe .
Kub@@ iba urwango
Ku ruhande rwe nka Perezida watowe , F√©lix Tshisekedi , yahisemo kuzahura umubano w' igihugu cye n' u Rwanda , mbere yo kohereza umubare w' ingabo za Congo mu Burasirazuba bw' igihugu ngo z@@ ijye kurwanya imitwe yitwaje intwaro yah@@ agize akarima kayo .
Ubu Ingabo za Congo ( FARDC ) zimaze kwigarurira ibice byinshi byari byar@@ ay@@ og@@ ojwe n' iyo mitwe ; ku buryo n' iyo gahunda yo kwigarurira ibice bya RDC iyo iza kuba ihari , icyizere cyayo ubu kiri kubar@@ irwa ku busa .
Abar@@ wanya ubutegetsi mu RDC bahisemo kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda n' Ab@@ anye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda kugira ngo bac@@ e intege umubano mwiza uri kubag@@ arirwa hagati y' u Rwanda na RDC .
Ariko n' ubundi abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi nta nyungu bafite mu kuba amahoro yagaruka muri RDC .
Mu myaka 25 ishize , ikibazo cy' umutekano muke mu Burasirazuba bwa RDC cy@@ afashije abari abami b' intambara kwigwizaho imitungo no kwinjira mu bikorwa bya politiki cyangwa igisirikare .
Urugero rwa hafi ni umutwe wa ADF - Nal@@ u ukomoka muri Uganda , wigize nka ba kavukire , ukaba uterwa inkunga n' uwahoze ari umunyapolitiki ku butegetsi bwa Kabila , M@@ busa Nyamw@@ isi , ubu wit@@ uriye muri Uganda .
Uyu M@@ busa Nyamw@@ isi yan@@ ahoze ari mu ihuriro L@@ amuka , nyuma aza kwitandukanya naryo .
Mu gihe RDC iri kugerageza kwivana mu ntambara imaze imyaka irenga 20 , cyane cyane hashingiwe ku mibanire myiza n' abaturanyi bo mu Burasirazuba , abarwanya ubutegetsi bakomeje kubiba urwango ku Banyarwanda , ariko si n' Abanyarwanda , ahubwo ni abo bita ko bakomoka mu bwoko bw' Abatutsi n' Ab@@ anye - Congo bavuga Ikinyarwanda mu rwego rwo guca intege umubano mwiza hagati y' u Rwanda na RDC .
Igitangaje ni uko imvugo ya " bal@@ kan@@ isation " ari ikirego kidafite ishingiro .
Mu gihe Umuhuzabikorwa w' Ihuriro ry' abatavuga rumwe n' Ubutegetsi , L@@ amuka , wan@@ ahoze ari Minisitiri w' Intebe , Adolphe Muz@@ ito , yagaragaje mu buryo bweruye ko ashaka gutera u Rwanda byan@@ ashoboka bakar@@ w@@ omeka kuri RDC ; uyu ni na we ushinja u Rwanda kugambirira kwigarurira ibice by' igihugu cye .
Nubwo bash@@ inje Joseph Kabila gufatanya n' u Rwanda muri uwo mugambi akiri ku butegetsi , ubu bakaba bageze kuri F√©lix Tshisekedi , ubwabo bigeze gukorana n' u Rwanda mu bihe byat@@ ambutse .
Ibi bigaragaza ikinyoma gikomeye kandi cy@@ umvikana .
Byongeye kandi muri gahunda y' ubuhahirane busesuye mu Muryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe n' ubusabe bwa RDC bwo kwinjira mu Muryango wa Afurika y' Uburasirazuba ( EAC ) , bigaragara ko kwigarurira ubutaka bw' ikindi gihugu byaba ari amafuti .
Aho gutanga ibisubizo by' ibibazo nyabyo Ab@@ anye - Congo bafite ubu nk' ubushomeri , kutagira inganda zihagije no kwangiza ibikorwa remezo , kwangirika kw@@ ' ibikorwaremezo n' ibindi bishobora gus@@ unikira urubyiruko rudafite akazi kwishora mu byaha cyangwa kwinjira mu mitwe yitwaje intwaro , [ ‚Ä¶ ] abatavuga rumwe n' ubutegetsi muri RD Congo bahisemo gushy@@ ushya imitwe y' abaturage babo bakoresheje
imitekerereze ishaje .
Guk@@ oma mu nkokora u Rwanda cyangwa ikindi gihugu cyo mu Karere ntiby@@ ongera umusaruro ; ntibir@@ ema imirimo kandi ntib@@ in@@ azana ubukungu .
Abavuga " bal@@ kan@@ isation " ntibigeze bak@@ and@@ agiza ikirenge ku mupaka uhuza u Rwanda na RDC , umwe mu iny@@ urwaho na benshi ku Isi ; ntibigeze byibura ban@@ umva ubuhamya bw' abagore bah@@ akorera ubucuruzi , bah@@ amb@@ ukira inshuro nyinshi ku munsi bashaka imibereho .
Ubukungu nyabwo bwa RDC ni abaturage bayo .
Muri Afurika yose , umutungo kamere ub@@ yarira inyungu ibigo mpuzamahanga biw@@ ubyaza umusaruro n' abayobozi bamwe na bamwe bahabwa ut@@ uv@@ ungukira n' icyizere cyo kubar@@ indira ubutegetsi bwabo .

Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rw' umuhanda .

Stade ya Rwinkwavu ni yo yubatswe bwa mbere mu Rwanda , iherereye mu Murenge wa Rwinkwavu mu Karere ka Kayonza , yubatswe iruhande rw' umuhanda .
Hirya yayo gato h@@ ahoze hac@@ ukurwa amabuye y' agaciro ndetse amateka yerekana ko ari ho hambere yac@@ uk@@ uwe mu Rwanda n' Ababiligi .
Ni stade abenshi bit@@ irira Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa [ Charles Leon Pierre ] watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu 19@@ 31 kugeza 1959 , bivugwa ko yakundaga kureba aho bakinira umupira w' amaguru cyane ko nawe yajyaga ac@@ ishamo akaw@@ ukina .
Umunyamakuru wa IGIHE yat@@ embereye kuri iyi stade aganira n' abakuru barimo Musafiri Kab@@ emba watang@@ iranye n' ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro mu Rwanda , uyu kandi yari ahari ubwo iyi stade yatangiraga kubakwa .
Kab@@ emba Musafiri ufite imyaka 102 yabwiye IGIHE ko igitekerezo cyo kubaka iyi stade cyag@@ izwe n' umuzungu w' umub@@ iligi nyuma yaho benshi mu basore bakoresh@@ waga mu bucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro i Rwinkwavu , mu masaha y' ikig@@ oroba basoje akazi batag@@ iraga ikindi kintu kibah@@ uriza hamwe .
Amateka agaragaza ko ubucukuzi bw' amabuye y' agaciro mu Rwanda bwatangiye mu 1930 - 19@@ 31 ubwo gas@@ egere@@ ti yav@@ umbur@@ waga mu birombe bya Rwinkwavu na Rut@@ ongo .
Ababiligi ngo bazanye abak@@ ongomani 300 barimo na Musafiri kugira ngo bafatanye n' abandi basore b' abanyarwanda kuy@@ acukura .
Uko Stade ya Rwinkwavu yubatswe
Kab@@ emba Musafiri avuga ko iyi stade ijya kubakwa yari ahari ariko ko at@@ ibuka neza umwaka , gusa ngo byaturutse ku muz@@ ungu w' umub@@ iligi wari umuyobozi mukuru w' abac@@ ukura amabuye y' agaciro ndetse akanaba inshuti y' Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Uyu muz@@ ungu yazanye umukino w' umupira w' amaguru nk' uburyo buzajya bufasha abac@@ ukuzi b' amabuye y' agaciro kwidagadura mu gihe bavuye muri iyo mirimo .
Ati " [ Stade ] yay@@ ishinze hafi mu 19@@ 40 , yashinzwe n' umuzungu w' umub@@ iligi wakundaga gukina umupira w' amaguru , Umwami Rudahigwa yarah@@ azaga cyane nawe ak@@ ishimira kubona uwo mukino , bigera aho bay@@ ishyiraho igipangu kiy@@ iz@@ engurutse hose , tway@@ ikin@@ ir@@ agaho nimugoroba no ku@@ cyumweru , ni nabwo Umwami yakundaga kuh@@ aza .
" Yari stade nziza cyane ifite igipangu , hari ikipe y' abac@@ ukura amabuye y' agaciro hakaba n' ikipe y' abazungu , hari n' andi makipe yadus@@ uraga ku cyumweru aturutse ahandi hantu hose bac@@ ukur@@ aga amabuye , amakipe yacu yose yabaga afite abajyanama .
Uko abakinnyi bah@@ embwaga
Kab@@ emba Musafiri yavuze ko abakinnyi batah@@ abwaga amafaranga ahubwo bahabwaga inka zabaga zatanzwe n' Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa .
Ati " Abakinnyi beza bahabwaga inka hamwe n' abatsinze ibitego , bab@@ anz@@ aga kubat@@ ekera neza bakah@@ aba ibiryo byinshi birimo inyama ubundi bakajya mu kibuga bamara gutsinda nanone bak@@ aba@@ bagira inka , undi witwaye neza nawe akag@@ abirwa inka akay@@ it@@ ahana " " " " .
Umwami Rudahigwa yac@@ ish@@ agamo agak@@ ina umupira
Kab@@ emba Musafiri yavuze ko Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa yari umwe mu bakundaga gukina no kureba uko bakina umupira w' amaguru , ngo rimwe na rimwe nawe yajyaga ac@@ ishamo akaw@@ ukina nubwo bitari cyane .
Ati " Hari ubwo yazaga inaha ak@@ izih@@ irwa nawe agak@@ ina , yajyaga mu ikipe y' abac@@ ukur@@ aga amabuye hamwe n' abandi batware , abazungu b' abab@@ iligi nabo bakajya mu ikipe yabo ubundi bag@@ akina gusa ntabwo byabag@@ aho kenshi .
Kab@@ emba yavuze ko guhera mu 1960 kuzamura imipira yaberaga kuri iki kibuga yatangiye kug@@ abanyuka ndetse abaturage batangira gusenya ur@@ up@@ angu bak@@ itwar@@ ira amabuye kugira ngo bay@@ ubak@@ ishe .

Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru w' Urugaga rw' Aband@@ itsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise ' Sinz@@ at@@ esha Agaciro Uw@@ ak@@ ans@@ ubije ' kijya mu mizi amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda .
Umwanditsi Hategekimana Richard , Umuyobozi Mukuru w' Urugaga rw' Aband@@ itsi mu Rwanda agiye kumurika igitabo gishya yise ' Sinz@@ at@@ esha Agaciro Uw@@ ak@@ ans@@ ubije ' kijya mu mizi amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda .
G@@ ikubiyemo amateka y' abagore mu Rwanda rwa mbere y' ubuk@@ oloni , gut@@ eshwa agaciro mu buk@@ oloni na nyuma y' aho ndetse n' uburyo bongeye gusubizwa agaciro nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Iki gitabo cy' amapaji asaga 250 kizam@@ urikwa ku mugaragaro kuwa Gatanu tariki 15 Ugushyingo 2019 muri Kigali Convention Centre .
H@@ et@@ egek@@ imana usanzwe yandika ibitabo bitandukanye , yavuze ko iki gitabo kigaragaza neza uburyo mbere y' umw@@ ad@@ uko w' abazungu abanyarwandakazi bagiraga ijambo mu miyoborere n' ubuzima bw' igihugu , bik@@ avaho mu gihe cy' ubuk@@ ool@@ oni , muri Repubulika ya mbere n' iya kabiri , bakongera kwisanga mu buzima bw' igihugu ubwo Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yah@@ agarik@@ waga n' Ingabo za FPR Inkotanyi zari
ziyobowe na Perezida Paul Kagame .
Muri iki gitabo atang@@ amo ingero z' uburyo abagore bagize uruhare mu rugamba rwo kubohora igihugu n' umusanzu bakomeje gutanga nyuma ya Jenoside ngo u Rwanda rw@@ ongere kuba igihugu cy@@ ubashywe .
Aganira na IGIHE , Hategekimana yavuze ko yanditse icyo gitabo , kugira ngo yibutse abagore ko ubwisanzure n' ijambo bafite hari aho byaturutse , bityo ko bakwiriye kurinda icyo gih@@ ango bafitanye na Perezida Paul Kagame .

Umusozi wa Kigali n' Igenamigambi ry' ingoma inye ( Ubu twag@@ ereranya na Vision 2020 cyangwa 2050 ) .
Kumenya icyerekezo cy' u Rwanda mu myaka ijana ni byo bitw@@ ereka neza icyo ubusugire n' ubwigenge by' u Rwanda gakondo byari bisobanuye , bityo na none tuk@@ abasha no gusobanukirwa neza n' icyari ku mutima ( Phil@@ os@@ oph@@ ie ) w' abakurambere bar@@ emye u Rwanda bakar@@ w@@ ubaka , bakar@@ urw@@ anira ndetse benshi bakan@@ ar@@ upf@@ ira .

Nk@@ ' uko mus@@ anzwe mubizi , mu mazina y' Abami atanu yas@@ imbur@@ anaga mu bihe bine yakurikir@@ anaga atya : Mutara , Kigeli , Mibambwe , Yuhi na Cyilima .
Aha biragaragara neza ko hagati ya Mutara na Cyilima hac@@ agamo Ingoma eshatu mbere y' uko Cyilima atangiza ikindi cyiciro cy' Abami .
Inshingano z' abami Kigeli na Mibambwe zabaga ari uk@@ wagura u Rwanda kuko ku ngoma eshatu zabaga zar@@ abanje Inka n' Abantu byabaga byarag@@ wiriye bityo hakaba harag@@ ombaga kuboneka uruh@@ um@@ ek@@ ero habayeho kwagura ubutaka bw' igihugu .
Yuhi yari ashinzwe imihango y' i Bwami cyane cyane Umuriro waho utar@@ azim@@ aga ukaba war@@ arang@@ aga ubusugire bw' igihugu .
Aha murumva ko Yuhi yari ashinzwe gutunganya ibijyanye n' ubusugire bw' igihugu n' ibijyanye n' imiyoborere myiza kimwe n' Iyobokamana kugira ngo abandi bami bane babone urufatiro rukomeye baz@@ ubak@@ iraho .
Ubwo hari aho bit@@ aniye cyane n' ibikorwa ubu mu igenamigambi rir@@ er@@ ire ?
Yaba Yuhi , Kigeli na Mibambwe uko ari batatu bab@@ anz@@ iriz@@ waga kandi bagah@@ eruk@@ wa na Mutara cyangwa na Cyilima .

Amah@@ ame remezo y' u Rwanda gakondo
Iyi mihango yakorwaga n' Abami bitwa Mutara na Cyilima hari ibintu idus@@ obanurira neza bigatuma tumenya Ih@@ ame - ngengabitekerezo ry@@ ubatse u Rwanda r@@ ikar@@ uha Ind@@ angagaciro .

Izo mbunda babahaye zigera ku 300 nizo z@@ abash@@ utse batangira kwig@@ erezaho ngo bagiye gutera u Rwanda rw@@ abaz@@ eng@@ ereje imyaka myinshi , dore ko hari ikindi gitero Rwabugili yari aherutse kubag@@ abaho mu myaka ibiri yari ishize , ni ukuvuga mu wa 18@@ 92 .
Bitewe nuko ibice byo mu Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda byari byar@@ amaze kwig@@ ar@@ urirwa burundu n' u Rwanda , icyari kir@@ aje ishinga Rwabugili , ni ibihugu byo mu Burengerazuba bw' u Rwanda byari bitar@@ igar@@ urirwa ibindi by@@ igar@@ uriwe n' abab@@ anjirije Rwabugili , byar@@ atangiye kwigomeka .
Abany@@ ank@@ ore bari batangiye kwiga uburyo bag@@ aba ibitero by' ubushotoranyi ku Rwanda , bikaba n' uburyo bwo kubih@@ im@@ uraho kuko bari barab@@ umv@@ ishije mu gitero cyah@@ erukaga .
Ubush@@ otoranyi bwakozwe na Ntare IV Rug@@ ingiza rwa Mig@@ ereka umwami wa Nk@@ ore wat@@ waraga icyo gihe , aho yamb@@ utse umupaka aza kuny@@ aga Iny@@ ambo z' i Rwanda , agat@@ wika ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rut@@ ar@@ aka muri Nyagatare .
Icyo gihe Rwabugili yari yarag@@ abye ibitero mu Burengerazuba bw' u Rwanda ku Ijwi ryari ryar@@ ig@@ ometse , ar@@ abimenya ko umwami wa Nk@@ ore Ntare Rug@@ ingiza rwa Mig@@ ereka yamuteye ak@@ anyaga Inka ze zari Rut@@ ar@@ aka muri Nyagatare .
Umug@@ enga wazo Kinyam@@ akara cya Nd@@ ezi ari na we wayoboraga ingoro ya Rwabugili yari i Rut@@ ar@@ aka mu Nd@@ orwa , yari mu ruzinduko , nuko bany@@ aga inka za Rwabugili n' umwe mu baj@@ a be barimo Nyir@@ anz@@ iza m@@ uka Mp@@ ore ya Sem@@ and@@ ira .
Umut@@ asi wabanje gut@@ atira Ntare yari umuhungu we Muh@@ anika wa Ntare .
Amakuru y' icyo gitero cy' Abany@@ ank@@ ore , Rwabugili yay@@ abar@@ iwe n' umuh@@ ima B@@ ukom@@ ang@@ ando w@@ abaciye mu rihumye ak@@ abonera ak@@ ito kuri ibyo bitero ko kwih@@ akirwa kuri Rwabugili , kuko yari amuz@@ iho ubuh@@ angange n' ubud@@ atsindwa .
Rwabugili uburakari bur@@ amusaba yibaza uko ari bub@@ ig@@ enze ab@@ ifatira ingamba , kuko ntabwo yagombaga kugaruka igitero cyo ku Ijwi atag@@ is@@ oje .
Yaje gutegura igitero cyagabwe ku Bany@@ ank@@ ore muri Gashyantare umwaka wa 18@@ 94 , cyiswe " Igitero cy' Imig@@ ogo " " " " kuko cyitabiriwe n' Imitwe ibiri y' Ingabo z' Abany@@ ank@@ ore zitwa : " " " " Ing@@ ogo n' imig@@ ogo " " " " .
Umwami Kigeli Rwabugili wari i Bun@@ yab@@ ungo n' Ingabo ze , yabanje kohereza yo Nyam@@ uh@@ enda wa Kaj@@ eje , n' umutwe yari ayoboye witwaga " Ibis@@ um@@ izi " " " " .
Mu gushy@@ ika aho urug@@ erero rw' Abany@@ ank@@ ore rwari ruk@@ ambitse i Kagitumba , Nyam@@ uh@@ enda wa Kaj@@ eje yasanze atari uk@@ uny@@ aga Inka gusa , ahubwo biteguye no kurwana .
Nyam@@ uh@@ enda n' Ibis@@ um@@ izi , bakabona Abany@@ ank@@ ore barimo bohereza mu kirere ibintu bit@@ urika by@@ aka umuriro bik@@ abay@@ obera kuko batari bagas@@ obanukirwa n' imikorere y' imbunda zari z@@ adutse vuba muri Afurika .
Bitewe nuko gusubira inyuma ku rugamba no kuruh@@ unga bitari mu ndangagaciro z' Abanyarwanda , biyemeje kur@@ urwana , nubwo babonaga harimo udushya twinshi turimo n' imbunda zitari z@@ imenyerewe muri aka karere .
Icyo gitero Abany@@ ank@@ ore bagabye mu Rwanda , nicyo kiswe mu mateka y' u Rwanda na Nk@@ ore " E@@ h@@ ururu ya Rwanda " " " " .
Urugamba rwar@@ emeye mu Kib@@ ande cya Ruh@@ umba rwa Kiyo@@ jo .
Nyam@@ uh@@ enda n' Ibis@@ um@@ izi yari ayoboye , Abany@@ ank@@ ore bah@@ abar@@ asira kubam@@ ara kuko bo bari bakir@@ wan@@ isha imih@@ eto n' imyam@@ bi , abandi bafite imy@@ uko iruka umuriro !
Nyam@@ uh@@ enda abonye ko Ingabo zigiye kumush@@ irana , ar@@ avun@@ ura ahagarika urugamba ajya guh@@ amagaza indi mitwe y' ingabo .
Nuko atanga ubutumwa ib@@ ukuru aho Rwabugili yari , amut@@ angariza amac@@ umu y' urugamba .
Rwabugili yaz@@ ibir@@ anyijwe n' uburakari butagira ingano , bitewe n' agasuzuguro kangana gutyo Abany@@ ank@@ ore bas@@ uzuguye u Rwanda none bakaba bagiye no gutsindwa urugamba rwo kubar@@ wanya , bitar@@ igeze bibaho mu mateka y' abami b' u Rwanda .
Rwabugili yafashe imitwe y' Ingabo yose yari ku Ijwi n' i Bun@@ yab@@ ungo yageraga kuri 30 , ah@@ amagaza n' indi yari iny@@ any@@ angiye ku ng@@ erero zitandukanye hirya no hino mu gihugu yose igera kuri 50 , bar@@ avun@@ ura batera Nk@@ ore .
Bageze i Rut@@ ar@@ aka ku ngoro ya Rwabugili , basanga har@@ abaye amat@@ ongo , bah@@ icara umwanya munini biga imigendekere y' urugamba bag@@ iyemo .
Abany@@ ank@@ ore babonye Ingabo z' uruv@@ ung@@ anz@@ oka z' Abanyarwanda , zitangiye kub@@ any@@ anyag@@ iramo , batangira gushya ubwoba , ariko bir@@ ema agatima ku bwo kwiringira imbunda bari bafite kandi bibwiraga ko Abanyarwanda bari bataragera ku ikoranabuhanga nk' iryo .
Abany@@ ank@@ ore batangira kurasa mu kirere no guk@@ anga kw@@ inshi , ariko Abanyarwanda barimo kub@@ iga no kwitegereza ibyo barimo .
Rwabugili ak@@ itegereza iyo my@@ uko yohereza imiriro mu kirere , niko kubaza Nyam@@ uh@@ enda wa Kaj@@ eje , ati " Ko ndeba bariya Bany@@ ank@@ ore bohereza imiriro mu kirere , kandi nkaba mbona igera ku butaka yaz@@ imye , bab@@ icishije iki ?
Nyam@@ uh@@ enda wa Kaj@@ eje , amut@@ ekerereza uburyo bagiye bakabah@@ agarara imbere bahanganye nk' abagiye kuras@@ ana nk' uko bisanzwe mu mir@@ w@@ anire ya gakondo , noneho batangira kubar@@ asa mu mutwe no mu gituza abantu batangira kw@@ ikubita hasi n' intwaro zabo , ari nako urush@@ unzi rw' amaraso rw@@ isuka ku butaka , bapfa umus@@ ubizo .
Mu gice gikurikira , tuz@@ abar@@ ambur@@ ira imigendekere y' urwo rugamba rw@@ ongereye ibigwi bya Rwabugili n' igit@@ inyiro cy' u Rwanda kir@@ ushaho kwiyongera ‚Ä¶ .
Nz@@ aharanira kutar@@ uta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa !
Isezerano rya Bamporiki nyuma yo kugirwa Minisitiri
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco .
Ku wa Mbere tariki 4 Ugushyingo 2019 nibwo Perezida wa Repubulika Paul Kagame yashyize mu murimo mishya bamwe mu bayobozi banyuranye .
Bamporiki Edouard yagizwe Umunyamabanga wa leta muri Minisiteri y' Urubyiruko n' Umuco .
Nyuma yo guhabwa uyu mwanya Bamporiki Edouard yashimiye Perezida Kagame amwizeza ko ataz@@ amut@@ enguha ndetse azas@@ ohoza ubutumwa amut@@ umye .
Abinyujije ku rukuta rwe rwa Twitter , Bamporiki yagize ati " W@@ itaba kare ugat@@ umwa kure , Wat@@ umwa n' Umukuru ug@@ ashima ush@@ ingura ugana iyo ut@@ umwe .
Ubutumwa mump@@ aye Nyakubahwa Mut@@ oza w' Ikirenga Paul Kagame nz@@ abus@@ ohoza bw@@ emye , nz@@ aharanira kutar@@ uta ubutumwa kuko buruta intumwa .
Nz@@ aba Mud@@ ah@@ usha ku ruh@@ embe munt@@ umye kuras@@ aniraho .
U Rwanda nir@@ wem@@ e .
Ubu butumwa buri mu Kinyarwanda cyiza , bw@@ umvikanisha uburyo uyu mugabo wari usanzwe ari umukuru w' Itorero ry' Igihugu yishimiye inshingano nshya yahawe .
Usibye kuz@@ ishimira , ikindi Bamporiki yav@@ uzemo ni uko atazigera ashaka kuruta ubutumwa ahawe kuko buruta intumwa .
Aha akaba y@@ umvikan@@ ishaga ko ataz@@ itwaza umwanya abonye ngo akom@@ ere kuruta inshingano ze .
Bamporiki yamenyekanye nk' umukinnyi wa filime , ikinamico akaba n' umwanditsi w' ibitabo , imivugo n' ibis@@ igo , azwi cyane mu ikinamico urun@@ ana aho akina yitwa Tad@@ eyo cyangwa se K@@ ide@@ yo , aho akina ari se wa Bud@@ ens@@ iyana na Sol@@ ina , inshuti ya Bush@@ ombe na Sit@@ ef@@ ano b' i Nyar@@ ur@@ embo .
Yavutse tariki 24 Ukuboza 198@@ 3 , i Nyamasheke mu Ntara y' Iburengerazuba , ari naho yaje kwiga amashuri abanza ndetse n' ayisumbuye , nyuma yiga amategeko mpuzamahanga muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK .
Yak@@ uze akunda cyane kwandika imivugo , bituma yitabira amarushanwa atandukanye mu bigo by' amashuri .
Afite imyaka 11 gusa y' amavuko , yakoze umuvug@@ o witwa " Iyo bad@@ ats@@ embwa tuba dut@@ w@@ enga " " " " ari nawo watumye amenyekana nk' umus@@ izi akiri umwana .
Amaze kuba umusore yagiye abona umwanya wo kuvuga imivugo mu birori bitandukanye byo ku rwego rw' igihugu , nko ku munsi mukuru w' Intwari n' indi minsi mikuru itandukanye .
Bamporiki wari usanzwe yumva ikinamico " Urunana " " " " akiri muto , akifuza kuba umwe mu bakinnyi bayo , mu 2003 yashak@@ ishije aho umushinga uy@@ itegura ukorera , arah@@ amenya maze agezeyo arab@@ inginga ngo bareke ajye akinamo .
A@@ za kub@@ yemererwa maze ahabwa umwanya yitwa Tad@@ eyo .
N ' ubwo abantu bagiye bumva Tad@@ eyo akina ari umusaza ndetse ufite abana bakuru n' abuzukuru , yari muto kuko icyo gihe yari afite imyaka 20 y' amavuko , bamwe mu bakinaga byumvikana ko ababereye umubyeyi baramur@@ ut@@ aga .
Mu bindi bijyanye n' ubuhanzi , Bamporiki yakunze kugaragara muri filime zitandukanye ndetse ahabwa ibikombe n' ibihembo muri sinema , haba mu z' abandi yagiye akinamo ndetse no mu zo yagiye yandika akan@@ az@@ ikinamo .
Muri z' abandi yagaragayemo harimo iyitwa ' Muny@@ ur@@ angabo ' y ' uwitwa Isaac Ch@@ ung ukomoka muri Amerika , iyitwa ' Rwanda t@@ ake two ' ya P@@ ia nawe wo muri Amerika , n' iyitwa ' Imit@@ oma ' ya K@@ wezi John .
Mu maf@@ il@@ ime yanditse ku giti cye akan@@ akinamo harimo iyitwa ' Ukuri kuri he ' ndetse na ' L@@ ong Co@@ at ' ( Ik@@ ote rir@@ er@@ ire ) .
Mu 2006 yitabiriye Iserukiramuco ry' amafilime rya C@@ ann@@ es mu Bufaransa , mu 2010 yitabira ir@@ yabereye i Rot@@ ter@@ d@@ am mu Buholandi , mu 2011 yitabira ir@@ yabereye muri Turikiya ryitwa " Crim@@ es and p@@ un@@ ish@@ ment " " " " .
Mu 2008 yabonye igihembo yakuye i New York muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , akaba yarah@@ emb@@ ewe kwandika filime nziza ( Best Sc@@ r@@ ip@@ t ) abik@@ esheje filime " L@@ ong Co@@ at " " " " , yagaragayemo abahanzi b' Abanyarwanda nka Nirere Shanel , Mani Martin n' umukinnyi Jimmy Gatete .
Mu 2011 yabonye igihembo cy' umukinnyi mwiza ( Best Act@@ or ) mu iserukiramuco rya He@@ art Land .
Nyuma y' ubuhanzi mu byiciro bitandukanye , Bamporiki mu 2013 yatorewe kuba intumwa ya rubanda , aba Umudepite mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y' u Rwanda .
Ku itariki ya 30 Kanama 2017 , Bamporiki yahawe imirimo mishya agirwa Umuyobozi w' Itorero ry' Igihugu .
Bamporiki ni umugabo wubatse , wam@@ bik@@ anye impeta y' urud@@ ashira na Uw@@ ingabire Claudine tariki ya 18 Ukuboza 2010 .
Bamporiki yize amasomo atandukanye , arimo ajyanye na sinema yize i Burayi ahitwa Pl@@ ag@@ ue , aza no kwiga muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ibijyanye no kubaka amahoro no kurwanya amakimbirane .
Mu masomo asanzwe yize muri Kaminuza yigenga ya Kigali ULK aho yakuye impamyabumenyi y' icyiciro cya gatatu mu mategeko mpuzamahanga .
Ubutumwa bwa Bamporiki Edouard nyuma yo guhabwa umwanya mushya

Inkomoko gakondo y' ibic@@ umbi by' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye n' ibic@@ umbi bikuru by' imiryango bakomok@@ amo nka gakondo y' ubutaka bw@@ atu@@ weho n' abakurambere mbere y' uko b@@ ororoka bag@@ akwirakw@@ ira hirya no hino ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , ari nako bab@@ uh@@ angaho ibihugu byaje k@@ ungwa bik@@ abyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Abantu benshi bakunze kwibaza ikibazo kijyanye n' ibic@@ umbi bikuru by' imiryango bakomok@@ amo nka gakondo y' ubutaka bw@@ atu@@ weho n' abakurambere mbere y' uko b@@ ororoka bag@@ akwirakw@@ ira hirya no hino ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , ari nako bab@@ uh@@ angaho ibihugu byaje k@@ ungwa bik@@ abyara igihugu kimwe aricyo u Rwanda .
Nk@@ ' uko tubikesha igitabo " Iy@@ ororoka ry' Abanyarwanda , Inkomoko y' imiryango migari " dukesha Umus@@ izi Nsanz@@ abera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu muco , ubus@@ izi n' amateka y' u Rwanda , tugiye kubat@@ ek@@ erere za gakondo nkuru z' ibic@@ umbi bikuru by' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda .
Abanyarwanda bibumbiye mu B@@ icumbi bikuru by' imiryango , imiryango migari ndetse n' inzu z' imiryango .
Ib@@ icumbi bikuru by' imiryango , nibyo by@@ abyaye imiryango migari , naho imiryango migari ibyara inzu z' imiryango .
Muri aya mateka tukaba tugiye kw@@ anz@@ ikira kuri gakondo z' ibic@@ umbi bikuru by' imiryango y' Abanyarwanda aribyo : Abas@@ inga , Abaz@@ igaba n' Abany@@ iginya .
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abas@@ inga
Abat@@ ekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abas@@ inga batuye bwa mbere ku butaka bw' u Rwanda , bafite inkomoko ku Bah@@ ima babarizwa ku butaka bw' igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abah@@ ima b' Abany@@ ank@@ ole " " " " .
Mu iy@@ aduka ryabo , baje bafite intego yo guhamya ubuh@@ angange bwo gutura ku butaka bwari but@@ w@@ ikir@@ iwe n' amashyamba ya kim@@ eza , bab@@ uh@@ angaho ibihugu , bituma bakura izina ryabo mu rurimi rw' igis@@ ekuruza cyabo rw' urun@@ yank@@ ore , bakur@@ ijeho kwitwa " Abas@@ inga " " " " aribyo mu Kinyarwanda bisobanuye : ' ' Abat@@ sinze " .
Mu gutura kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda , Abas@@ inga binj@@ iriye bwa mbere mu Majyaruguru y' u Rwanda bakom@@ ereza mu Burengerazuba bagana mu Majyepfo , bakurikiranye ubut@@ ohe bw' umw@@ eg@@ ega w' Ikiyaga cya Kivu n' amashyamba y' Ibir@@ unga n' aya kim@@ eza nka Gishwati , Nyungwe , Mukura na Cyam@@ ud@@ ongo .
Ayo mashyamba bayah@@ ereyeho bahiga , kugeza ubwo ba@@ yat@@ utira , bayah@@ angaho ibihugu .
Kubera ko ntawe bac@@ uran@@ waga ngo abak@@ ome imbere kuri ubu butaka , bar@@ isanzuye barat@@ ura kugeza n' ubwo bas@@ akaje ingoma zabo mu Rwanda rw' u Burengerazuba , mu Rwanda rw' Amajyepfo no mu Rwanda rwo Hagati ndetse bambuka na Nyabarongo bas@@ atira u Rwanda rw' i Burasirazuba .
Gakondo yabo ari nayo gic@@ umbi gikuru batuyemo , kuri ubu ni mu Mirenge ya : Kig@@ eyo , Mush@@ onyi , Mus@@ asa , Ruhango , Gih@@ ango , Kiv@@ umu na Bon@@ eza yo mu Karere ka Rutsiro n' Umurenge wa Nyamy@@ umba wo mu Karere ka Rubavu
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abaz@@ igaba
Abat@@ ekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda , bagaragaza neza ko Abaz@@ igaba batuye mu ba mbere kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda bakurikiye bene wabo b' Abas@@ inga , bafite ikom@@ oko ku Bah@@ ima babarizwa ku butaka bw' igihugu cya Uganda , aribo bakunze kwita " Abah@@ ima b' Abany@@ ank@@ ole " " " " .
Mu iy@@ aduka ryabo , baduk@@ iriye igice cy' i Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda b@@ og@@ oze ibiyaga bigari bih@@ abarizwa , aba ariho bat@@ ema amashyamba ya Cy@@ im@@ eza baray@@ ak@@ onda , baray@@ at@@ utira bayah@@ angamo ibihugu bishyira kera .
B@@ atuye ako gace bab@@ ungira ubut@@ ohe g@@ akom@@ ora ku ruzi rw' Akagera n' ibiyaga bih@@ aboneka nka N@@ asho , H@@ ago , Ih@@ ema n' ibindi .
Nuko batangira kwagura ibihugu byabo bagana mu Rwanda rwo hagati no mu Majyepfo y' Iburasirazuba .
Gakondo y' imb@@ anza y' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abaz@@ igaba ni mu mirenge ya : Mw@@ ili na Mur@@ undi yo mu Karere ka Kayonza , ukongeraho Umurenge wa Rw@@ imbogo yo muri Gatsibo .
Gakondo z' igicumbi gikuru cy' imiryango y' Abany@@ iginya
Abat@@ ekereze b' amateka y' Ig@@ icumbi cy' imiryango migari cy' Abany@@ iginya , bavuga ko cyaba gikom@@ oka mu Majyaruguru y' Iburasirazuba bwa Afurika mu gihugu cya Ethiopia .
Inkomoko yabo ikaba ari iyo mu muryango w' Abag@@ ala bakunze kwita n' Abar@@ omo , wari ukomeye muri icyo gihugu kandi wari nawo mug@@ abw@@ angoma mu myaka ya 300 nyuma ya Yezu Kirisitu .
Abany@@ iginya bas@@ esekaye mu Karere ka Afurika y' Iburasirazuba no mu Rwanda , ah@@ asaga m@@ uwa 700 , ubwo bari mu iy@@ imuk@@ ayim@@ uka nk' abandi bose ry' abatuye muri Afurika , bashaka ubw@@ inyag@@ ambur@@ iro bw' imiryango yabo n' amatungo yabo .
Nyuma y' igihe kitari gito , bafashe urugendo rwo mu muhora uhuza Afurika y' Amajyaruguru y' Iburasirazuba n' iy@@ ' Amajyepfo , bag@@ aca mu bihugu bya Somaliya , Kenya na Uganda , niko gus@@ esekara kuri ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda .
Bar@@ as@@ ukiye mu Burasirazuba bw' u Rwanda mu Murenge wa Gatsibo wo mu Karere ka Gatsibo , basanga Abaz@@ igaba barah@@ ak@@ abye bar@@ ema ingoma y' u R@@ we@@ ya rw' u M@@ uba@@ li , yari ikom@@ atanyije Imirenge y' Akarere ka Gatsibo , n' imirenge imwe n' imwe iri mu Majyaruguru y' Akarere ka Kayonza .
Abah@@ as@@ esekaye muri ibyo bihe , nibo bav@@ uyemo Abas@@ ekuruza b' Im@@ banza ba K@@ azi wabyaye Gihanga cyah@@ anze ingoma y' u Rwanda .
Mu gus@@ esekara mu R@@ we@@ ya rw' Abaz@@ igaba , bah@@ as@@ eruk@@ anye , ibigwi n' imihigo y' ibyo bazanye muri aka karere , nk' uko bab@@ ivuze mu izina ryabo ubwo Abaz@@ igaba babaz@@ aga izina ryabo .
Nk@@ ' aho bak@@ avuze ir@@ y' igis@@ ekuruza cyabo cy' Abag@@ ala cyangwa se Abar@@ omo , baduk@@ ana izina rishya ry@@ ibigwi n' ibirindiro by' ahazaza habo , ry' Abany@@ iginya rish@@ atse kuvuga " Abantu bar@@ ambye ku butunzi n' ubupf@@ ura " " " " .
Nyuma y' imyaka isaga 300 , Abany@@ iginya bamaze mu bus@@ em@@ bere bacumbikiwe n' Abaz@@ igaba , nibwo umucyo w' ubuh@@ angange w@@ abam@@ urikiye bahanga igihugu cyabo kit@@ waga Gasabo , cy@@ injira mu ruhando rw' ibindi bihugu bigera kuri 24 byari bis@@ anganyije ubu butaka bw' u Rwanda , baba babaye igihugu cya 25 , gih@@ angwa na Gihanga Ngom@@ ijana , umuk@@ ur@@ ambere w' Abang@@ iy@@ inya bahanze ingoma y' u Rwanda .
I Gasabo niho Abany@@ iginya n' imiryango i@@ bakom@@ okaho bag@@ uriye ubutaka bwabo bahanga ibindi bihugu ku bis@@ igara by' ubutaka Abas@@ inga n' Abaz@@ igaba bari baran@@ ennye .
Ibihugu byah@@ anzwe na bene Gihanga , muri byo dus@@ angamo Nd@@ orwa y' Abash@@ ambo , Kiba@@ li y' Abega , u Bug@@ ara bw' Aba@@ cyaba n' u Bugesera bw' Abah@@ ond@@ ogo .
Amateka y' imp@@ itab@@ ie ku gihugu cy' u Rwanda , adut@@ ekerereza ko gakondo nkuru y' igicumbi gikuru cy' Abany@@ iginya n' imiryango migari i@@ bakom@@ okaho , ari mu Mirenge ya Nduba , Bumbogo , Rut@@ unga , Gikom@@ ero , Ndera na Rusororo yo mu Karere ka Gasabo , ukongeraho n' Umurenge wa F@@ umb@@ we wo mu Karere ka Rwamagana .
Nyuma yo kubagezaho Gakondo nkuru z' ibic@@ umbi by' imiryango y' Abanyarwanda , mu bice bik@@ urikiraho , tuz@@ abagezaho za Gakondo nkuru z' imiryango migari y' Abanyarwanda , uko ari 24 .
Imp@@ an@@ uro zikubiye mu gitabo " Amakosa 100 nt@@ icuza " " " " cya Ruba@@ duka Frank
Ruba@@ duka Frank yanditse igitabo kigaragaza amakosa yakoze mu buzima ariko at@@ icuza .
Iki gitabo yacy@@ ise ' 100 m@@ ist@@ ak@@ es i d@@ on@@ ' t reg@@ r@@ et ' cyangwa se mu rurimi rw' Ikinyarwanda ' Amakosa 100 nt@@ icuza ' .
Ruba@@ duka Frank yanditse igitabo kigaragaza amakosa yakoze mu buzima ariko at@@ icuza .
Iki gitabo yacy@@ ise ' 100 m@@ ist@@ ak@@ es i d@@ on@@ ' t reg@@ r@@ et ' cyangwa se mu rurimi rw' Ikinyarwanda ' Amakosa 100 nt@@ icuza ' .

Village Urugwiro , inyubako y' amateka akomeye mu Rwanda
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako y@@ ubashywe kuva icy@@ ubakwa kugeza n' ubu .
Benshi tuy@@ ir@@ ebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuy@@ igomba nk' ibiro bicur@@ irwamo icy@@ erecyezo git@@ umye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko y' amahoro aduh@@ esha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Village Urugwiro , ni inyubako y@@ ubashywe kuva icy@@ ubakwa kugeza n' ubu .
Benshi tuy@@ ir@@ ebera kure kubera icyubahiro tuy@@ igomba nk' ibiro bicur@@ irwamo icy@@ erecyezo git@@ umye u Rwanda ruba ubukombe , ikaba isoko y' amahoro aduh@@ esha ibikombe mu mahanga .
Ni inyubako y' amateka kuko abagera kuri 50 % by' Abanyarwanda bariho bavutse iriho , ig@@ anje ku Kacyiru , mu Karere ka Gasabo mu Mujyi wa Kigali aho imaze imyaka 44 .
Y@@ ubatswe mu 197@@ 5 n' Umuryango wahuzaga Ibihugu bya Afurika cyane cyane ibyak@@ olon@@ ijwe n' u Bufaransa n' ib@@ ikoresha Igifaransa , Organiz@@ ation Commun@@ e Afric@@ aine et Mal@@ g@@ ache ( O@@ CA@@ M ) .
Uwo muryango kuri ubu waz@@ imye , u Rwanda rw@@ aw@@ injiyemo mu 196@@ 5 .
Mu 197@@ 5 , nibwo rwari kwakira inama yawo yagombaga kwitabirwa n' abakuru b' ibihugu bagera kuri 15 .
Byari ihurizo rikomeye ku gihugu nk' u Rwanda cyari gifite hoteli nke zitwa ko zikomeye nka Mille Collines na Diplomate zari zigezweho icyo gihe ariko zifite ubushobozi bwo kwakira abashyitsi bar@@ inganiye .
Muri icyo gihe u Rwanda rw@@ iteg@@ uraga kwakira inama , inyubako za mbere za Village Urugwiro zubatswe ku mafaranga ya O@@ CA@@ M nkuko Rucagu Boniface , umwe mu bagize Urwego Ng@@ ishwanama rw' In@@ araribonye yabibwiye IGIHE .
Inama ya O@@ CA@@ M irangiye , inyubako za Village Urugwiro z@@ eguriwe Leta y' u Rwanda nayo izih@@ ind@@ uramo hoteli yakiraga abifite muri ibyo bihe .
Nubwo Village Urugwiro yabaye hoteli , mu gihe u Rwanda rw@@ abaga rwakiriye inama zikomeye yakomezaga kwifashishwa mu kwakira abashyitsi ba Leta .
Urugero ni tariki 21 na 22 Gicurasi 1979 ubwo u Rwanda rwak@@ iraga inama ya Gatandatu ihuza u Bufaransa na Afurika yan@@ itabiriwe na Perezida wari uyoboye u Bufaransa icyo gihe , Val@@ √©@@ ry Marie Ren√© Georges Gis@@ card d@@ ' Est@@ a@@ ing .

Uwo mwaka ni nabwo hubatswe hoteli Nov@@ ot@@ el Umubano ( Mar@@ asa Umubano Hotel kuri ubu ) nabwo ku mafaranga yatanzwe n' u Bufaransa .

Kur@@ asaga , imy@@ ots@@ o , kur@@ um@@ ika , kug@@ ombora : Uburyo gakondo bwam@@ amaye mu kuvura indwara z' amayobera
K@@ urum@@ ika no kur@@ asaga , imy@@ ots@@ o no kug@@ ombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uw@@ abikor@@ aga akaba afite imy@@ erere y' uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikan@@ avura .
K@@ urum@@ ika no kur@@ asaga , imy@@ ots@@ o no kug@@ ombora , ni imigenzo nyarwanda yakorwaga mu buvuzi gakondo no kurinda ibyago Abanyarwanda , bityo uw@@ abikor@@ aga akaba afite imy@@ erere y' uko iyo bikozwe byanze bikunze birinda kandi bikan@@ avura .
Gusa kuri ubu Abanyarwanda benshi ntibaby@@ emera , ndetse bavuga ko ari imihango ya gip@@ agani , n' ubwo hari abaganga bemeza ko iyo migenzo yabaga ari ingirakamaro .
Nk@@ ' uko tubikesha igitabo " Umuco mu B@@ uv@@ anganzo " cyanditswe n' Umus@@ izi Nsanz@@ abera Jean de Dieu , Inzobere ku muco , amateka n' ubuv@@ anganzo nyarwanda , tugiye kubat@@ at@@ urira imwe mu mihango n' imigenzo yakorwaga mu kuvura no kurinda indwara mu muco w' Abanyarwanda .
Kur@@ asaga ( Guca ind@@ as@@ ago , guk@@ eba gahoro gahoro ku mubiri ) umuntu byat@@ erwaga n' uko bashaka nko kum@@ ushyiramo imiti yo kum@@ uvura ikintu arwaye , cyangwa kum@@ uts@@ irika bavuga ngo bataz@@ amur@@ oga , bakar@@ asaga rero bag@@ ashyiramo iyo miti .
Hari n' aho bik@@ engeraga ko umwana wavutse azahura n' akaga , nako bakag@@ ats@@ irika bakoresheje kumuca ind@@ as@@ ago , ukaz@@ asanga koko bibaye impamo , ibyago bak@@ etse , akab@@ icika .
Hari kandi n' ind@@ as@@ ago bac@@ aga ku mugore ugiye gushaka cyangwa umugabo , bag@@ ashyiramo imiti ituma bahamya umubano uzira kid@@ obya .
Niyo mpamvu uzasanga abantu bakuru benshi bafite ind@@ as@@ ago ku mubiri , ku gik@@ anu , mu gatuza , ku bib@@ ero ku gahanga , mu biganza n' ahandi .
Umum@@ aro w' ind@@ as@@ ago ahanini , wari uwo guts@@ irika ushyiramo umuti aho baras@@ aze , bak@@ ung@@ ikanya n' imit@@ ongero runaka yo kuvura , imit@@ ongero ig@@ akurwa n' indi maze umuntu akaba mut@@ araga .
K@@ urum@@ ika ho bac@@ aga ind@@ as@@ ago nko mu gik@@ anu cyangwa mu mugongo , bagashyiraho ikintu bita ing@@ unga .
Ing@@ unga kari agac@@ uma bak@@ ebye kat@@ agira ijosi .
K@@ urum@@ ika babikor@@ aga bashaka gusohora amaraso mabi ari mu mubiri .
Hari nk' ubwo imitsi y@@ ipfund@@ ik@@ aga ikab@@ uza umuntu kuba yagenda , ugasanga aho y@@ ipfund@@ itse habaye nk' umukara , uwo byabayeho agakunda kugira ib@@ inya bim@@ ufata bya hato na hato .
Bar@@ as@@ ag@@ aga ya maraso agas@@ ohoka , nyuma bagas@@ ig@@ amo imiti yo kugira ngo h@@ om@@ oke h@@ asub@@ irane , ariko na none ig@@ akiza ubwo burwayi ntib@@ uz@@ agaruke .
Hari n' aho bar@@ um@@ ik@@ aga bakoresheje ihembe rik@@ iy@@ omeka ku mubiri rik@@ ajya rik@@ urura amaraso , ryam@@ ara kuzura bak@@ arik@@ uraho bakay@@ am@@ ena bakongera bag@@ asub@@ izaho .
Kur@@ asaga no kur@@ um@@ ika , bifite itandukaniro benshi badakunze kumenya .

Nyuma y' imyaka 300 yo gusahura Afurika abaturage bayo bajyanwa ku ngufu mu mirimo y' agahato n' ubucakara muri Amerika , mu 188@@ 4 Abany@@ aburayi bahinduye umuv@@ uno noneho bajya umugambi wo kugira Afurika iy@@ abo .

Iyo nama yamaze amezi atatu kuko yarangiye tariki 26 Gashyantare 188@@ 5 , ibihugu byose bimaze kwemeranya uko biz@@ igabanya Afurika , by' umwihariko iby@@ ifat@@ aga nk' ibikomeye birimo u Budage , u Bufaransa , u Bwongereza , u Buholandi , u Bubiligi , Portugal na Espagne .

Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwir@@ akwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma w' u Rwanda , Ros@@ alie Gic@@ anda yishwe n' ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , az@@ izwa ko ari umututsi .
Tariki 20 Mata 1994 nibwo inkuru mbi yakwir@@ akwiye ko umwamikazi wa nyuma w' u Rwanda , Ros@@ alie Gic@@ anda yishwe n' ingabo za Leta yakoraga Jenoside , az@@ izwa ko ari umututsi .
Gic@@ anda yashakanye n' Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa Charles L√©on Pierre Kuwa 13 Mutarama 194@@ 2 .
Y@@ abayeho nabi as@@ uz@@ ugurwa nyuma y' urupfu rw' umwami Rudahigwa , ubwo yatangiraga i Bujumbura ku buryo bw' amayobera tariki 25 Nyakanga 1959 .
Nyuma yo gutanga kw@@ ' umugabo we by@@ ajyanye n' ih@@ urura ry' abarw@@ aniraga Repubulika , ariko barushaho gutesha agaciro ingoma ya Cyam@@ i n' ibimenyetso byayo .
Mu 196@@ 1 Perezida Kayibanda Gr√©g@@ oire yirukanye mu ruk@@ ari Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda .
Yaje gutura mu Mujyi wa Butare mu Karere ka Huye , ari naho abahoze ari abasirikare ba Habyarimana hamwe n' Interahamwe bamusanze bakamw@@ ica kuwa 20 Mata 1994 .
Urupfu rw' Umwamikazi Ros@@ ali Gic@@ anda
Muri Repubulika ya mbere n' iya kabiri , umwamikazi Gic@@ anda nubwo yari mu gihugu , yabayeho nta gaciro afite nk' uwahoze mu buyobozi bukuru bw' igihugu .
Gic@@ anda wari umuyoboke ukomeye wa Kiliziya Gatolika , yabayeho mu buzima bw@@ oroheje mu mujyi wa Huye , abana n' umubyeyi we ndetse n' abandi bagore bake bam@@ ufashaga mu mirimo itandukanye .
Ubwo Jenoside yatangiraga , Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda yagiye y@@ ishingikiriza Jean Baptiste Habyarimana wari Perefe wa Butare , war@@ wanyije cyane umugambi wo gutsemba Abatutsi .
Tariki 17 Mata , Perefe Habyarimana yatawe muri yombi , nyuma aza kwicwa .
Umwamikazi Ros@@ alia Gic@@ anda yatangiye guterwa ubwoba ko nawe agiye kwicwa n' umuryango we .
Raporo ya Human Rights Watch yasohotse mu 1999 , ivuga ko Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda wari ufite imyaka 66 yasabye Joseph Kany@@ aba@@ shi wari Burugumesitiri wa Komini ya Ngoma i Butare kumurinda , undi akaby@@ anga .
Tariki 20 Mata ahagana saa tanu z' amanywa , abasirikare bayobowe na Lt Pierre Bizimana binjiye mu rugo rw' umwamikazi Gic@@ anda ku mabwiriza yari yatanzwe na Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana wari umuyobozi ushinzwe ubutasi n' ibikorwa mu ishuri rikuru rya gisirikare , ES@@ O ubwo Jenoside yakorwaga .
Abo basirikare bamaze kwinjira mu rugo rw' umwamikazi , baram@@ ufashe we n' abandi bagore batandatu babanaga bar@@ abatwara .
Muri urwo rugo hasigaye mama wa Gic@@ anda wari ufite imyaka 80 n' undi mukobwa wo kumwitaho .
Abasirikare bafashe Gic@@ anda n' abo bari bafatanywe bajyana inyuma y' ingoro y' inzu ndangamurage y' u Rwanda bar@@ abar@@ asa , barapfa .
Ku gicamunsi abasirikare bagarutse mu rugo rwa Gic@@ anda gusahura , hashize iminsi ibiri bar@@ agaruka bica umubyeyi we .
Raporo ya H@@ uma Rih@@ g@@ ts Watch ivuga ko hari umupadiri wasabye ko umubiri wa Gic@@ anda w@@ ashyingurwa mu cyubahiro , bur@@ ugumesitiri Kany@@ aba@@ shi yohereza abagororwa bo kuw@@ ujyana baw@@ ushy@@ ingura hafi y' urugo rwe .
Umwe mu baganiriye n' umukobwa wabashije kurokoka wit@@ aga ku mubyeyi wa Gic@@ anda , ngo yamubwiye ko mbere y' uko Gic@@ anda n' abo bari kumwe bicwa babanje kuvuga isengesho bishyira mu maboko y' Imana .
Muri 2012 , urukiko rwashyiriweho u Rwanda rwakatiye Capt Ildephonse Nizeyimana igifungo cya burundu ashinjwa kwica Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda n' abandi batutsi muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Nizeyimana yari yafatiwe muri Uganda mu 2009 .
Mu 1998 Lt Pierre Bizimana yakatiwe urwo gupfa n' urukiko rwa gisirikare i Kigali ariko icyo gihano kiza guhind@@ urwamo igifungo cya burundu nyuma y' uko u Rwanda ruk@@ uyeho igihano cy' urupfu .
Umwamikazi wic@@ ishaga bugufi , akagira impuhwe
Abab@@ anye n' abazi neza Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda , bavuga ko yari umubyeyi wic@@ isha bugufi kandi agakunda abantu bose atar@@ obanuye .
Mu buhamya Perezida Paul Kagame yatanze mu 2017 avuga ku mateka y' ubuto bwe kuva afite imyaka ine y' amavuko ubwo yatangiraga ubuzima bw' ubuhunzi , yashimiye na Gic@@ anda nk' umwe mu bamufashije akabasha kurokoka .
Ubwo buhamya bugaragara mu nimero 29@@ 44 ya Jeune Afrique yasohotse ku wa 11 Kamena 2017 , yiswe amabanga y' ubuto [ Sec@@ ret@@ s de Jeunesse ] bw' abakuru b' ibihugu barimo Perezida Kagame , Ali Bongo Ond@@ imba , Umwami Mohammed VI wa Maroc na Alpha Cond@@ √© .
Perezida Kagame yasobanuye ko mu 196@@ 1 mbere gato y' uko u Rwanda rubona ubwigenge , ubwo yari afite imyaka ine , Abahutu bari batuye ku musozi wa T@@ ambwe bashy@@ igikiwe n' ubuyobozi , big@@ abije aho umuryango we wari utuye batw@@ ika inzu zaho ndetse bagirira nabi Abatutsi .
Icyo gihe umubyeyi we yatangiye kumut@@ egura ngo bah@@ unge .
H@@ ahise haza imodoka , umushoferi wayo ashyikiriza umubyeyi wa Perezida Kagame ibaruwa ivuga ko at@@ umwe n' Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda wari utuye i Nyanza mu rugendo rw' iminota nka 45 uvuye aho bo bari batuye .
Ros@@ alie Gic@@ anda yari amusabye kubah@@ ung@@ isha muri ibyo bihe by' amakuba .
Perezida Kagame n' abantu bari baturanye binjiye muri iyo modoka mu gihe igih@@ ir@@ iri cy' aba@@ bah@@ igaga cyat@@ urukaga ku wundi musozi , gihita cy@@ irara mu byo bari batunze .
Icyo gihe ngo basanze Umwamikazi i Nyanza , mbere y' uko bafata inzira bak@@ erekeza mu Mutara aho naho ubwicanyi bw@@ abas@@ anze bakab@@ uh@@ ungira muri Uganda .
Gic@@ anda yavukiye i Rwamagana mu 19@@ 28 .
Yak@@ uze arangwa n' ikinyabupfura ari nabyo byatumye ab@@ eng@@ ukwa n' Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa .
Umwamikazi Gic@@ anda aruh@@ ukiye i Mw@@ ima ya Nyanza ahat@@ abar@@ ijwe Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa na Kigeli V Ndahindurwa .
Buri mwaka tariki 20 Mata hategurwa gahunda yo kwibuka Umwamikazi Ros@@ alie Gic@@ anda , itegurwa ku bufatanye bw' umuryango we n' ubuyobozi bw' Ikigo cy' Igihugu cy' Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage z' u Rwanda .
Ibig@@ wi n' ibirindiro : Amateka n' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda ( Igice cya mbere )
Abat@@ ekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' aba@@ yat@@ eker@@ erezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafati@@ weho ibintu byinshi mu mateka y' u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Abat@@ ekereza b' amateka y' u Rwanda n' aba@@ yat@@ eker@@ erezwa , bakunze gutangaza byinshi ku mateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda rugari rwa Gasabo , inka yafati@@ weho ibintu byinshi mu mateka y' u Rwanda no mu ruhando mpuzamahanga .
Muri iki gice tugiye kubav@@ ungur@@ iraho gato ku big@@ wi n' ibirindiro by' amateka y' ibigwi by' inka mu Rwanda , dore ko ut@@ abik@@ uyeho akam@@ anyu nibura gato gato , ut@@ ashobora kub@@ iva im@@ uzi ngo ub@@ igere im@@ uz@@ ingo .
Nk@@ ' uko tubikesha igitabo " Intwari z' imb@@ anza , zubatse u Rwanda rug@@ ahamya igit@@ inyiro " cyanditswe n' Umus@@ izi Nsanz@@ abera Jean de Dieu , inzobere ku M@@ uco , ubus@@ izi n' amateka , tub@@ imburiye ku iy@@ injira ry' inka mu Rwanda n' uko zat@@ ejwe imbere zikaba urufatiro rukomeye rw' ibintu byinshi mu mateka .
Inka ifite ibis@@ ekuruza byinshi mu mateka y' Afurika , aho bisaga imyaka 3000 .
Inka zah@@ anganywe n' u Rwanda , aho z@@ aduk@@ anywe n' Abas@@ ang@@ wab@@ ut@@ aka b' Abas@@ inga n' Abaz@@ igaba ah@@ asaga mu wa 300 .
Abany@@ iginya bah@@ as@@ esekaye , bateje imbere cyane ubworozi bw' inka bituma inka zose zo mu gihugu baz@@ itirirwa , aho mu mateka bagira bati " Gihanga niwe wah@@ anze inka n' ingoma " .
B@@ ikom@@ oye ku kuba Abany@@ iginya aribo bahaye intera ndende n' urwego rw' ikirenga ubworozi bw' inka , ziba nyinshi mu gihugu .
Inka yahawe intera iy@@ ing@@ ay@@ inga iy@@ ' umuntu .
Aho mu B@@ ucur@@ abwenge bw' inka , bagiraga bati " Inka ni imfura , kuko upfa ik@@ akur@@ erera , wab@@ umbira ( wabura amashereka ) ik@@ akug@@ oboka , ik@@ ak@@ urw@@ anyiriza indwara z' ibyorezo n' ubuj@@ yah@@ abi " " " " .
Inka niyo yar@@ angaga ubukire , Inka niyo yari ipfundo ry' ubuh@@ ake nk' akazi ko hambere , Intwari yo ku rugamba yag@@ oror@@ erwaga inka , Inka yung@@ aga inshuti , Inka yah@@ uzaga inshuti ( abah@@ anaga inka , babaga babaye inshuti ) , Inka bayik@@ waga umugeni nk' ikimenyetso cy' uburere bwiza .
Mu Kin@@ yejana cya Mun@@ ani nyuma ya Yezu , ni ukuvuga ah@@ asaga mu wa 700 , nibwo hadutse ishyanga rishya mu Rwanda , ari ryo ryaje kuvamo umuryango mugari w' Abany@@ iginya , baza n' ubundi , bag@@ owe n' iy@@ imuk@@ ayim@@ uka ryabo n' umutungo wabo urang@@ ajwe imbere n' inka bagendaga bash@@ akira inz@@ uri zit@@ oshye kandi ng@@ ari .
Mu gus@@ esekara mu Rwanda , binj@@ iriye bwa mbere mu Gihugu cy' u R@@ we@@ ya rw' u M@@ uba@@ li ( mu mirenge ya Mur@@ undi na Mw@@ ili yo mu Karere ka Kayonza na Rw@@ imbogo yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo ) .
Kuko ubutaka bub@@ ereye ubworozi bw' inka zabo bari bab@@ ug@@ ezeho , bishimiye umuk@@ enke w' Iburasirazuba bw' u Rwanda , ug@@ arag@@ iwe n' ubut@@ ohe bw' umur@@ ambi w' ubutaka bwig@@ anjemo icy@@ og@@ ogo cy' uruzi rw' Akagera , ibiyaga bya Rwany@@ akiz@@ iga , N@@ asho , Ih@@ ema n' ibindi .
Imyaka isaga 300 ( 700 - 10@@ 91 ) , umuryango mugari w' Abany@@ iginya wamaze mu bus@@ em@@ bere mu ngoma y' u R@@ we@@ ya rw' Abaz@@ igaba , nta kindi cyera cyangwa se cy@@ ir@@ abura bakoze , usibye guteza imbere ubworozi bw' inka , bakora ubug@@ enge n' ubuhanga bwo kuz@@ ib@@ angurira kugira ngo zir@@ usheho k@@ ororoka , maze nazo zir@@ abak@@ undira zir@@ or@@ oka karahava ! !
Aha akaba ari naho , bakuye umwihariko w' inka zit@@ irirwa u Rwanda z' Iny@@ ambo aribyo bivuga " It@@ ungo ry' int@@ or@@ anywa " .
Imis@@ ozi yose bac@@ umbik@@ iwemo , yari yiganjemo inz@@ uri z' inka , aho gutura ari hato , ku buryo aribo ba mbere bateje imbere gutura mu ns@@ isiro mu rwego rwo kurinda akajagari mu mit@@ urire byari kugabanya ingano y' inz@@ uri z' inka zabo .
Mu misozi batuyemo myinshi kuri ubu ibarizwa mu Karere ka Gatsibo ¬æ byayo byari inz@@ uri z' inka .
Muri yo twavuga Imis@@ ozi ya Nyag@@ ih@@ anga , Rugarama , Ng@@ arama , Kabarore , Git@@ oki , Gatsibo na Kag@@ eyo
Imis@@ ozi batuyemo muri ibyo bihe , ari nayo barem@@ yemo ins@@ isiro , ni mu mu Murenge wa Remera na Muh@@ ura yo mu Karere ka Gatsibo .
Uko imyaka yash@@ iraga indi ig@@ ataha , niko Abany@@ iginya barush@@ agaho guteza imbere ubworozi bw' inka , ari nako butuma bagira ijambo ry' icyiz@@ er@@ abuh@@ ake mu R@@ we@@ ya , kugeza ubwo by@@ abah@@ esheje ijambo mu nzu y' ubwami bwabo , ban@@ ashak@@ amo abagore b' ibikom@@ angoma .
Muri bo twavuga nka Nyir@@ aruk@@ angaga rwa Nyam@@ ig@@ ezi ya Kab@@ eja , wash@@ atswe na K@@ azi ka Kiz@@ ira , bakab@@ yarana Gihanga .
Abany@@ iginya bakomeje kug@@ wiza ubutunzi bw' inka , amash@@ yo n' amagana , bibaha imbaraga n' icyubahiro cy' ikirenga , kugeza ubwo ibwami batangiye kubak@@ eka am@@ ababa ko bashobora kuz@@ abamb@@ ura ingoma , ari nabwo Gihanga yab@@ imeny@@ aga agashyira nzira akabah@@ unga ajya guhanga igihugu cye mu bis@@ igara by' ubutaka Abas@@ ang@@ wab@@ ut@@ aka ban@@ ennye , akab@@ uh@@ angaho igihugu cy' i Gasabo .
Gihanga , akimara guhanga Gasabo , Umuryango mugari w' Abany@@ iginya akomokamo akaw@@ ukura mu bus@@ em@@ bere mu ngoma y' u R@@ we@@ ya , yashyizeho igenamigambi ry@@ eruye rishingiye ku nka mu kubaka igihugu cye .
Inka ihabwa umwanya ukomeye mu buzima bwose bw' igihugu , aho yifash@@ ishwaga muri Politiki z' igihugu zitandukanye nko mu B@@ ubanyi n' amahanga , mu kubaka ubukungu bw' igihugu , mu mutekano no mu ntambara zo kwigarurira amahanga , mu mibereho myiza y' abaturage , mu mibanire n' ubumwe bw' abenegihugu n' ibindi .
Inka yay@@ ishyize mu ig@@ amigambi ry' ububanyi n' amahanga n' ubutwererane n' abami b' ibindi bihugu bit@@ uranyi by' u Rwanda ku buryo yagombaga guhuza u Rwanda n' ibihugu by' inshuti kandi ikag@@ abirwa abami b' ibihugu byanga u Rwanda , bityo bikag@@ abanya urwango , ubundi ruk@@ abasha gukora ibikorwa by' iterambere rwifuza .
Inka yabaye inkingi ya mwamba yo kurwanya umwanzi w' imbere mu gihugu .
Umwanzi w' imbere mu gihugu , burya ni ubukene .
Iyo umunyarwanda atak@@ ennye , nta nabi agira , kandi umwanzi wo hanze y' igihugu ntiy@@ abona aho yinj@@ irira , kuko uw@@ akam@@ ubereye icy@@ itso wo mu gihugu hagati , baba bar@@ amug@@ ushije ruh@@ abo .
Nuko Gihanga , agena gahunda zo kug@@ abira abaturage inka ku buntu , kugira ngo biteze imbere , ubundi amahoro ah@@ inde mu miryango yabo .
Inka yashyizwe mu rwego rwo gufasha igihugu mu kugera ku mutekano n' intwaro yo guhashya amahanga adakunda u Rwanda .
Niho Gihanga , yah@@ ereyeho ashyiraho gahunda yo kug@@ abira inka Ingabo zose z' igihugu , kugira ngo zir@@ usheho kwitabira intambara zo kwiv@@ una abanzi , no kugira im@@ bad@@ uko ku rugamba rwo kwagura igihugu .
Inka yafati@@ weho umurongo mugari wo kwigarurira imitima y' abaturage b' ibindi bihugu u Rwanda rw@@ ashakaga kwigarurira .
Aho buri muturage u Rwanda rw@@ abaga rw@@ any@@ aze mu bitero byo kur@@ wagura , yahabwaga inka nyinshi zo korora zik@@ amufasha kwikura mu bukene , bityo akinjira muri Paradizo nshya y' igihugu cy' u Rwanda , irimo amata n' ubuki , umutima akaw@@ ukura kuri gakondo y' iwabo , akag@@ anza i Rwanda .
Gahunda yo kug@@ abira abaturage b' ibindi bihugu bany@@ azwe n' u Rwanda , yatumye benshi mu baturage bator@@ oka ibihugu byabo , biy@@ izira mu Rwanda , bahabwa inka zo korora , ubundi batangira gutanga amakuru y' im@@ bamut@@ ima y' uburyo u Rwanda ruz@@ igarurira ibihugu bakomok@@ amo .
Ubukungu bw' ibihugu mu bihe byo hambere , bwari abaturage ku isonga , ubundi butunzi bug@@ akurikiraho , ari nayo mpamvu u Rwanda , rwih@@ atiye kwigarurira abaturage b' ibindi bihugu , rw@@ ifashishije inka .
Impamvu igitabo kid@@ akwiriye kubura mu mpano uha uwo ukunda
Mu buzima bw' umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kim@@ un@@ eza , kim@@ uk@@ emurira ibibazo , kim@@ uteza imbere ndetse kin@@ amw@@ ubaka .
Mu buzima bw' umuntu bwa buri munsi , akenera kugura ikintu akeneye kim@@ un@@ eza , kim@@ uk@@ emurira ibibazo , kim@@ uteza imbere ndetse kin@@ amw@@ ubaka .
Abantu bamwe baha agaciro kad@@ akwiye igitabo , ntibazi ko igitabo aricyo shingiro ry' iterambere rirambye , ishingiro ry' ubuzima bwiza , ishingiro ry' ubwenge , ishingiro ry' imibereho myiza , ishingiro ryo kubaka igihugu , ishingiro ryo gusigasira igihango ndetse igitabo ni ishingiro ryo kugira igenamigambi rirambye .
N@@ jya nibaza ibibazo bikurikira : Kuki umuntu agura umwenda w' ibihumbi ijana ariko akumva at@@ agura igitabo cy' ibihumbi ijana ?
Kuki umuntu agura mudasobwa y' ibihumbi magana atanu ariko akumva at@@ agura igitabo cy' ibihumbi magana atanu ?
Kuki umuntu agura urur@@ abo rwo guha inshuti ye ariko akaba at@@ amuha impano y' igitabo ?
Mu mwaka wa 2016 , hari inshuti yanjye yitwa K@@ en Char@@ tr@@ and twigeze kuganira turi gutembera i New York , ambwira ko mu mpano nziza ashobora guha umuntu akunda ko h@@ adashobora kubur@@ amo igitabo , m@@ ubajije impamvu arambwira ngo igitabo ni inshuti nziza muganira uk@@ unguka ubwenge n' ubuhanga , kikaba urwibutso rur@@ ambye kandi rud@@ ashira .
K@@ en yambwiye ko igitabo ari urwibutso rw' ubushuti , ko buri kwezi agura ibitabo bibiri byo gusoma kandi ko adashobora kuryama adas@@ omye igitabo kuko gituma aruhuka neza , ak@@ unguka ubumenyi bur@@ ushijeho .
Nyuma y' ikiganiro twagiranye , nahise nkunda bir@@ ushijeho igitabo , mpitamo kwimakaza umuco wo kwandika , kugura ndetse no gusoma ibitabo .
Kugeza ubu maze kwandika ibitabo bine .
Mu biro byanjye harimo ibitabo nag@@ uze ns@@ oma kenshi , mu rugo umuryango wanjye n@@ awug@@ uriye ibitabo byo gusoma kandi bamaze kubik@@ unda .
Bir@@ akwiye ko tw@@ imakaza uyu muco mwiza ufasha kubaka u Rwanda twifuza ndetse n' Afurika , tug@@ ura ibitabo , tub@@ iha agaciro gakomeye , tub@@ itang@@ amo impano ku nshuti dukunda , tub@@ isoma aho turi hose , bityo biz@@ adufashe kurushaho gutera imbere dufite ubuhanga bwimbitse .
Ibi kandi bizadufasha kwihuta mu iterambere ndetse turusheho kumenya aho tuva , aho tugeze ndetse n' icyerekezo cy' u Rwanda na Afurika .
Biz@@ adufasha kurushaho kuba abarinzi b' ibyagezweho mu Rwanda no muri Afurika bityo tub@@ isig@@ asire ndetse tun@@ aby@@ ubak@@ ireho ibindi bikorwa byinshi kandi byiza .

Imiryango yahamije ubuh@@ angange mu mateka : Ig@@ icumbi cy' Umuryango w' Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka
Mu mateka y' abakurambere mp@@ ang@@ arwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ik@@ avugwa cyane ku bw' ibigwi n' ibirindiro yabaga yar@@ akoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikom@@ ok@@ amo .
Mu mateka y' abakurambere mp@@ ang@@ arwanda , hari imiryango yagiye ihamya ibirindiro , ik@@ avugwa cyane ku bw' ibigwi n' ibirindiro yabaga yar@@ akoreye igihugu , hagati mu muryango mugari ikom@@ ok@@ amo .
Muri iki gice tukaba tugiye kub@@ imburira ku mateka y' igicumbi cy' umuryango mugari ufite inkomoko ku Mwami Yuhi Mazimpaka twifashishije igitabo " Iy@@ ororoka ry' Abanyarwanda , inkomoko y' imiryango migari " dukesha Umus@@ izi Nsanz@@ abera Jean de Dieu , inzobere mu Bus@@ izi , Umuco n' Amateka y' u Rwanda .
Yuhi III Mazimpaka ni mwene Sek@@ ar@@ ongoro Gis@@ anura cya Kigeli Nyam@@ uh@@ esh@@ era , Umun@@ yig@@ inya wo mu nzu y' Abag@@ anzu na Nyam@@ ar@@ embo ya Maj@@ inya , ukomoka mu muryango mugari w' Abak@@ ono , wategetse ah@@ asaga mu wa 16@@ 42 kugeza mu wa 16@@ 75 .
Ni umwami wa 18 muri 28 bategetse u Rwanda , akaba n' umwami wa 18 mu B@@ erekeza 34 b' umushinga wo kubaka u Rwanda , kugeza ubwo aya mateka yandik@@ waga .
Izina rye ry' ubutwari ryari " Ins@@ arik@@ an@@ amak@@ uza .
Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ni umwe mu B@@ ami b' u Rwanda bagize inzu z' imiryango nyinshi ugereranyije n' abandi bami , akaba akurikira Nd@@ oba na we wagize inzu z' imiryango nt@@ abarika .
Amateka atug@@ aragariza ko Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka ya Gis@@ anura , yabyaye abana benshi , biganjemo abahungu 10 barimo Rwaka , Ruj@@ ugira , Nyar@@ w@@ aya , G@@ akom@@ ba , Mur@@ eg@@ anshuro , G@@ apf@@ izi , Muk@@ ungu , Muk@@ uku , Rush@@ ara na B@@ ukom@@ be .
Umuryango w' Umwami Yuhi Mazimpaka w@@ abayemo ingabo z' ibik@@ ong@@ ote ku ngoma ye n' iy@@ ' umuhungu we Cyilima Ruj@@ ugira wam@@ uz@@ unguye ku ngoma .
Ban@@ abaye abag@@ aba b' ingabo b' int@@ ah@@ usha mu gihe cye .
Imitwe y' Ingabo yat@@ war@@ waga n' abahungu be , irimo Ind@@ ara zat@@ war@@ wag@@ wa na Muk@@ ungu wa Yuhi Mz@@ impaka ,

Abany@@ abug@@ eni b' abagore bahawe umwihariko mu kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga w' Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage
U Rwanda rur@@ itegura kwifatanya n' Isi mu birori by' Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage uz@@ izihizwa hatang@@ izwa imurika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni by' abahanzi b' abari n' abat@@ egarugori .
U Rwanda rur@@ itegura kwifatanya n' Isi mu birori by' Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage uz@@ izihizwa hatang@@ izwa imurika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni by' abahanzi b' abari n' abat@@ egarugori .
Buri mwaka tariki 18 Gicurasi Isi yizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wahariwe Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage , haz@@ irik@@ anwa umuco , amateka n' imibereho gakondo by' abatuye Isi .
U Rwanda narwo rw@@ ifatanya n' amahanga mu kwizihiza uwo munsi ushim@@ angira agaciro ko guhererekanya amateka no guteza imbere umuco ufatwa nk' umusingi w' imibereho y' igihugu .
U@@ rwa Gasabo r@@ ubarizwa mu Muryango Mpuzamahanga w' Ingoro Nd@@ angam@@ urage ( I@@ COM ) uh@@ uriyemo abanyamuryango basaga 44 000 bakora mu ngoro ndangamurage 20 000 zo mu bihugu 13@@ 8 .
Muri uyu mwaka , uyu munsi wahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga ku kugira " Ingoro ndangamurage zigamije uburinganire , ubudasa no kudah@@ eza " .
Kuri iyi nshuro iki gikorwa cyateguwe mu buryo bwihariye aho haz@@ ifashishwa ikoranabuhanga bitewe n' ingamba zashyizweho zo guhangana n' ikwirakwira ry' icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Ni muri urwo rwego Ingoro ndangamurage zo mu bihugu bin@@ yamuryango bya I@@ COM zasabwe kucy@@ izihiza hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Ikigo cy' Ingoro z' Igihugu z' Umurage w' u Rwanda ( IN@@ M@@ R ) cyiz@@ izihiza ibi birori h@@ afungurwa ku mugaragaro imurika rishya mu Ngoro y' Ubug@@ eni n' Ubuh@@ anzi iherereye i Kanombe , ku wa 18 Gicurasi 2020 .
Iri murika ry' ibihangano by' ubugeni ryahawe insanganyamatsiko ivuga iti " Ubutumwa bw' abany@@ abug@@ eni b' Abanyarwandakazi : Uburinganire kuri bose .
Ni insanganyamatsiko yari yagenwe ku Munsi Mpuzamahanga w' Abari n' Abat@@ egarugori [ yasubitswe kubera ingamba zo guhangana na Coronavirus ] , ariko in@@ ahur@@ irana n' iy@@ atanzwe na I@@ COM uyu mwaka wa 2020 .
Iyo urebye mu byiciro bitandukanye bibar@@ izwamo abari n' abat@@ egarugori mu Rwanda , usanga baragize uruhare mu bikorwa by' iterambere ry' ubukungu n' imibereho myiza y' abaturage nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ; ariko basigara inyuma mu bijyanye n' ubugeni bitewe n' impamvu zirimo ubushobozi buke , kubura amahugurwa ahagije mu bijyanye n' ubugeni n' izindi mbogamizi zo mu buzima busanzwe .
Ush@@ ingiye no ku bihangano bimur@@ itse mu Ngoro y' Ubug@@ eni n' Ubuh@@ anzi y' i Kanombe " Hari icyuho kinini hagati y' ibihangano by' abagore n' abagabo .
Ibi ntibis@@ obanuye ko badashoboye , bafite impano muri bo kuko na bake bari muri uwo mwuga bakora ibihangano byiza cyane , bimwe muri byo bifite ubwiza burenze ibya basaza babo .
Im@@ urika riz@@ akorwa nk' uburyo bwo gukora ubukangurambaga mu bari n' abat@@ egarugori , binyuze mu butumwa bukubiye mu nsanganyamatsiko y' imurika no mu bihangano byabo byateguwe kandi bizam@@ urikwa , bakangurirwa kwigirira icyizere , gutinyuka no kugaragaza impano bafite mu by' ubugeni .
Iri murika ryateguwe hagamijwe gufasha abah@@ anzikazi bato no kubah@@ arurira inzira zo kung@@ ukira mu bikorwa byabo ; gufasha abany@@ abug@@ eni b' abagore gutegura ibikorwa byo kumurika ibihangano byabo ; kwerekana agaciro ko gushora mu bushobozi bw' umugore no kubafasha kugeza imishinga yabo ku rwego mpuzamahanga , byan@@ afasha abandi kubig@@ iraho .
R@@ izahuza abany@@ abug@@ eni b' abari n' abat@@ egarugori 35 bo mu bihugu bitandatu birimo u Rwanda , Amerika , u Bufaransa , u Bubiligi , Serbia na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
IN@@ M@@ R yateguye iri murika ifatanyije n' Ikigo Nd@@ angam@@ uco cy' Abadage Go@@ et@@ he Institut - Kigali .
Ibyo bigo byombi byafashije abari n' abat@@ egarugori b' abany@@ abug@@ eni mu kur@@ itegura , kubaha amahugurwa n' ubushobozi bwo gukora ibihangano byabo no gutunganya imurika r@@ iboneye .

Amakipe ashobora kongera gusubukura imyitozo ?
Nk@@ ' uko no mu bindi bihugu birimo iby@@ ' i Burayi biri gukorwa muri iyi minsi , hari ibyiciro bac@@ amo mu kongera gusubukura ibikorwa by' imikino .

Hari icyo byafasha amakipe yitegura amarushanwa
Lomami Marcel utoza Gorilla FC yo mu cyiciro cya kabiri izakina imikino ya Play@@ off@@ s yo guhatanira kuzamuka mu cyiciro cya mbere , yabwiye IGIHE ko nyuma y' amezi atatu imikino imaze ihagaze hari abakinnyi biyongereye ibiro ku buryo baramutse bemerewe gusubukura imyitozo hubahirizwa gusiga intera hagati y' abantu , hari icyo byafasha amakipe .
